Current Commentary

Personal Views on Building the Western Xinjiang Railway 9

According to previous reports, Central Committee member Fu Rulin has a plan to build the Western Xinjiang Railway. The route is planned to run from Xi'an directly to Yili in Xinjiang. Construction will begin as soon as the entire Longhai Railway is completed. It is said that the Longhai Railway can be completed in June of this year. If this plan can be continued, the transportation between Xinjiang and the interior can be opened up. However, Fu's proposal was sent down by the Executive Yuan to the four departments of Railways, Communications, Finance, and Industry for consultation, but no concrete results have been seen. It is difficult to predict what the future holds.

Our country today has many things waiting to be done. However, due to financial constraints, construction should be planned as a whole and priorities should be set. No one can deny this principle. However, careful consideration should be given to what should be done first and what can be delayed. In recent years, the government has paid increasing attention to transportation, especially aviation and highways. However, given the size of our country, the past achievements are difficult to be satisfied. From the perspective of politics, economy, and population distribution, the construction of the Western Xinjiang Railway is a matter of urgency. First, Xinjiang is located between the two great powers of Britain and Russia. Since the September 18th Incident, Russia has had designs on northern Xinjiang, and Britain has had designs on southern Xinjiang. Almost all the turmoil in the province in recent years is related to this international background. Moreover, Xinjiang has a complex ethnic makeup. Han Chinese and Hui people account for less than one-third of the population. The rest are the Uighurs, whose race and culture are very different. They often call for "reviving the Uighurs and destroying the Han." If we do not make plans early, things will become increasingly difficult in the future. Since the completion of the Turkestan-Siberia Railway, the situation in Xinjiang has become very dangerous. It is estimated that 80% of its products are absorbed by Soviet Russia, and it is increasingly isolated from our interior. This is a case of the guest dominating the host. Our country can only sit by and watch the situation develop and cannot take any action because it is beyond our reach. If we can build a railway from Xi'an directly to Yili and Tacheng, and build three or four branch lines to connect the north and south of Xinjiang, then even if something happens, the central army can be quickly transferred. Internal turmoil can be prevented, and external troubles can be reduced. This is one reason why the Western Xinjiang Railway should be built from a political perspective.

Furthermore, from the perspective of economic benefits, building a railway is also essential for developing Xinjiang. For example, the gold in the Altai Mountains is as important as that in Outer Mongolia and Heilongjiang. Only when it can be mined can it be used to support our country's conversion to the gold standard. Coal deposits in Dihua, Yili, and Suiding are everywhere and are second only to those in Shanxi. Other resources such as crude oil, copper, iron, jade, and stone are abundant and cannot be quantified. The Yili area also has forests stretching for hundreds of square miles, which can make up for our country's losses in Jilin. The silk and agricultural products in Hotan and Shule in southern Xinjiang are similar to those in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. As long as the railway is open, we can adjust the surplus and deficiency with our interior. This is the second reason why the Western Xinjiang Railway should be built from an economic perspective.

According to the results of the investigation by Professor Tawney, an economic historian at the University of London, who came to China in 1930, most of China's population is concentrated in the middle and lower reaches of the three major river basins. The coastal areas are particularly densely populated, which is very uneven compared to the sparsely populated border areas. We further examine the population situation in the coastal areas and find that their density is actually higher than in most countries. For example, Japan has always said that its population is too large and invades everywhere. In fact, the average population of its mainland is only 4,078 per square mile, while the coastal provinces of our country are far above that. For example, the average population of Shandong is 614 people per square mile, Zhejiang is 657 people, Jiangsu is 896 people, the Taihu Lake area is as high as 6,000 people, the Chengdu Plain reaches 2,000 people, and the lower reaches of the Pearl River are also very densely populated. From this point of view, our population surplus is actually more pressing than that of Japan. Shouldn't we start solving this problem earlier? The three northeastern provinces have always been the end of the northern population declaration. After the September 18th Incident, they have been forcibly occupied by Japan. The Nanyang area and Manchuria restricts the activities of overseas Chinese, which is very strict and difficult to develop. Today, to solve the population problem in the coastal provinces, the most appropriate way is to arrange for them to settle in the northwest. Xinjiang's area is 15 times larger than Zhejiang's, but its population is only 2.5 million, which is less than a corner of Shanghai. Its sparseness is evident. If the Western Xinjiang Railway becomes a reality, then all the surplus population, with the government's assistance, can be sent to Xinjiang as pioneers of development. The banditry caused by the overpopulation and difficult life in the coastal areas can be reduced. There is nothing better than this to achieve multiple goals at once.

As for how to carry out the construction, there are two points to consider: labor and funding. Our country has more than one million soldiers. Apart from fighting in civil wars, they can be said to be doing nothing. If we want to talk about reducing the military, they will become bandits and cause even greater harm. The best plan for now is to use them to build roads. After the roads are built, they can be used for reclamation and to defend against bandits. They can also engage in farming and animal husbandry. In this way, the military can be reduced without actually reducing it. This principle can be adopted for the construction of the Western Xinjiang Railway. The main line of the road runs for more than 6,000 li from Xi'an to Tacheng, and it would be a million li to build a circular Xinjiang line. Calculated at a price of three yuan per li, it would require 400 to 500 million yuan. Our country's financial strength will definitely not be able to bear such a huge amount of money. However, the total amount of domestic debt we have issued over the years has also reached hundreds of millions of yuan. If there is really no way to raise the money, and we have to consider the next best option, then it is not impossible to borrow foreign debt. However, it must not harm China's sovereignty. The country from which the loan is borrowed must be one that is not geographically adjacent, so as to prevent it from using the excuse of protecting the road to occupy the entire territory and turning into a continuation of the Northeast.

With the suppression of the Fujian Incident and the reduction of banditry, the unification of the country is beginning to take shape. If all parties can cooperate sincerely and keep the country and the nation in mind, broaden their horizons, and strive for construction for the sake of consolidating the border, then the achievements will be more than just the development of Xinjiang. Even the recovery of the lost territories in the Northeast will not be too difficult.

Rajchman to Return to Geneva on Schedule 10

Chen Zongcheng Will Also Go

(Nanjing) League of Nations technical expert Rajchman was summoned back to Geneva by telegram because the League of Nations Executive Council meeting was scheduled to be held in Geneva on May 16. Rajchman is scheduled to leave China by ship on the 10th of this month to return to Geneva. This trip is solely for reporting on his work in China and has no other tasks. The date of his return to China will depend on whether there is a need for him to come to China. (1st dispatch)

He is scheduled to leave Hong Kong by ship for Geneva on the 14th of this month. This trip will take approximately four months, and he will return to China in early August. (1st dispatch)

Internal Affairs Ministry Anniversary Celebration 11

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Internal Affairs held a celebration on the morning of the 1st to commemorate its sixth anniversary. Deputy Ministers Gan Naiguang and Fu Rulin, officials, and guests totaling more than 700 people attended. Gan Naiguang presided over the meeting and reported on the ministry's establishment and recent policy implementation. A luncheon was held for all staff at 4:00 p.m., and an entertainment program was held at 7:00 p.m. (1st dispatch from the Central News Agency)

Yutian's Surplus Police, Carrying Weapons, Harass the Zunhua-Fengrun Area 12

After Clashing with the Local Militia, They Return to the Yutian Border

New Security Brigade Commander

Han Dianbang Officially Takes Office Yesterday

(Tianjin) Surplus police from the Yutian Security Brigade, refusing to be dismissed, fled with weapons to the Zunhua-Fengrun border area to occupy it. On the 29th, one team fled to the Yankou of Zunhua, clashed with the local militia, and had four killed and two wounded. The rest could not break through and returned to Yutian. The new Yutian Security Brigade Commander, Han Dianbang, officially took office on the 1st and began using his official seal. Yin Rugeng originally planned to go to supervise the ceremony, but because he had to wait for Yu Xuezhong in Beiping, County Chief Chen Baofeng represented him instead. The long-distance telephone line from Zunhua to Tongxian, which was installed by the War Zone Industry Revitalization Committee, at the cost of hundreds of days of effort, officially opened on the 1st. (1st dispatch)

Yuguan Telegraph Bureau Still Controlled by Japanese Telegrams 13

(Tianjin) The telegraphs of Luandong can now reach Qinhuangdao. The Yuguan Telegraph Bureau is still being controlled by the Japanese puppet regime and refuses to return it, so we are still unable to directly report to that city. The puppet country's Ministry of Finance is implementing a unified currency system. All old issues of Fengpiao and Jihei official bills issued by Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang are limited to exchange by June. Merchants' account books are also being changed to the puppet Central National Currency standard. The puppet Jihai Railway Bureau has been abolished, and the railway has been renamed the puppet Jingtulu, i.e., the Jihui Railway branch line. (1st dispatch)

Airline Companies Merge 14

(Nanjing) The Sino-American China National Aviation Corporation and the Sino-German Eurasia Aviation Corporation have decided to merge to save costs. The Eurasia office in Nanjing will be transferred to the China National Aviation Corporation office starting on the 1st. The original location on Four Alleys is not sufficient for office space, and a new location has been found at Xinjiekou. They will move into the new location to work within days. (1st dispatch)

Han Fuqu Discusses the Imminent Annihilation of Liu's Bandits 15

(Jinan) Han Fuqu stated that Liu's bandits fled south from Tangdigou this morning and arrived at Luomidian, 30 li north of Juxian City, where they were intercepted by Kang Regiment of Gu Liangmin's Division. The battle was fierce, with more than 100 bandits killed. They fled southwest again, and were intercepted again at a fort 20 li northwest of the city. They then fled northwest to the south of Sibulizhai, where they were intercepted by Wu Yuanxing Regiment of Sun Tongxuan's Division. A fierce battle lasted for about an hour, with more than 100 bandits killed and more than 300 captured. Many guns, donkeys, mules, horses, and camels were obtained. The bandits' supplies were completely abandoned. The captured bandits have been ordered to be executed on the spot. The infantry bandits have all been dealt with. The remaining 450 cavalry bandits fled to Xiazhuang, 60 li southwest of Zhecheng. Gu's division immediately pursued them. The bandits saw the car and fled southeast again to Dadian Town, 25 li away. The troops are still surrounding and pursuing them on all sides, and it will not be difficult to annihilate them. This battle was the first time Liu's bandits had suffered a major setback in years. He no longer needs to depart because there are not many bandits left. He has ordered Zhan Shutang's division to return to defense. Two technicians from the Central Air Force arrived in Jinan today. The plane is scheduled to be flown to Jinan tomorrow morning by Captain Yang Yafeng. (1st dispatch)

(Qingdao) Lu and Han traveled to Bo on a special train on the 31st to personally supervise the suppression of Liu Guitang to thoroughly eliminate him. (1st dispatch)

Xu Yuanquan and Others Arrive in Hankou to Meet Zhang Xueliang 16

(Hankou) Xu Yuanquan and Zhang Fang arrived in Hankou by plane on the 1st from Shashi and Nanyang, respectively, to meet Zhang Xueliang, report on the affairs of the Yangtze River, and seek instructions on bandit suppression. Xiao Zhichu, Hao Mengling, and Tang Shanzhai also arrived here one after another. He Chenjun is scheduled to go to Jiangxi with Zhang Fang on the 3rd to meet Chiang. (1st dispatch)

(Hankou) He Zhuguo and Chief of Staff Yu Jianzhang, Director He Jinghua, and a dozen others went to Huangma in eastern Hubei on the 1st to inspect. Pang Bingxun arrived in Hankou on the 1st from Zhumadian to meet Zhang Xueliang, He Chenjun, and others. Wang Yizhe has already gone south and made a short stop in Xinyang. He is expected to arrive in Hankou on the 2nd. (1st dispatch)

(Hankou) Remnant bandits of the Pseudo 6th Division in the border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui fled to Wujia Town in Lishan. Xiao Zhichu sent troops on the 28th to defeat them. They retreated to Yangtianwo and are being pursued. (1st dispatch)

He Yingqin and Huang Shaoxiong Exchange Opinions on Mongolian Affairs 17

He Plans to Resign as Director of Guidance

Huang Leaves Beiping for Taiyuan to Meet Yan

(Beiping) He Yingqin and Huang Shaoxiong exchanged views on the Mongolian issue for a long time this morning. London Silver Agreement Approved by Six Countries

Spain and Peru Have Not Approved

(Washington) Tomorrow is the deadline for countries to approve the London Silver Agreement. According to Senator Pittman, leader of the Senate silver bill, the countries that have approved the agreement are the United States, Mexico, Canada, India, China, and Australia. However, there have been no reports of approval from Spain and Peru to date. Some view this as an indication of Spain and Peru's opposition to approving the agreement. Senator Pittman is the initiator of the London Silver Agreement and the vanguard of other silver bills. According to Pittman, the non-participation of Spain and Peru does not hinder the materialization of the agreement. Pittman's reason is that Spain and Peru's position in the world economic conference is relatively unimportant and easily absorbed by other countries. Today, advocates of using silver as currency stated that the content of the London Silver Agreement is clear and accurate, which is its advantage. Moreover, many silver-using countries can propose practical limits to bind themselves without any hesitation. India has now approved the agreement, so in the next four years, India will sell approximately 140,000,000 ounces of silver. Beyond this limit, India can also sell silver to the United States to pay war debts, but the total amount must not exceed 176,000,000 ounces. China has also acknowledged that it will no longer sell silver obtained from melting silver coins within four years. The London Silver Agreement stipulates that the United States will purchase 114,000,000 ounces of newly mined silver annually for a period of four years, and the value of each ounce of silver will be 64.5 cents (US). When the London Silver Agreement was drafted, there was an understanding among the countries that if the agreement was not approved by the proposed countries by April 1, 1934, silver-producing countries would be restricted, except for silver-using countries. (31st National Telegram)

Oldest German Newspaper Ceases Publication 22

Founded 230 Years Ago

(Berlin) Germany's oldest newspaper, the Vossische Zeitung, founded 230 years ago, has now ceased publication. A notice was issued today stating that, given the current state of national affairs, the newspaper's mission has been completed. At the same time, five other newspapers published in Hamburg have been forced to close due to financial difficulties. One of them, specializing in commercial and shipping news, was established in 1730 and was also one of Germany's famous newspapers. (31st Reuters Telegram)

Japan Opposes Second Washington Conference 25

Advocates Individual Meetings

Adjusting Far East Issues

(Nanjing) Foreign Minister Hirota mentioned the Manchurian problem and the issue of guaranteeing Pacific security in his note to US Secretary of State Hull on February 21, expressing his intention to begin consultations between Japan and the United States in the form of mutual agreements prior to the naval disarmament conference. However, in his reply to Foreign Minister Hirota on March 3, Secretary of State Hull avoided the aforementioned Japan-US consultations. The United States' intention to convene a conference of countries related to the Nine-Power Treaty has caused dissatisfaction in various circles in Japan. The Nine-Power Treaty is intended to protect the interests of so-called countries in the Far East, and it clearly does not include "Manchukuo." Therefore, Hull's intention seems to be to convene a second Washington Conference to discuss the Manchurian problem. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' intention is to disregard Secretary of State Hull's true intentions, but to absolutely oppose the conference of countries related to the Nine-Power Treaty, and to consistently advocate the following individual agreements to resolve the necessary issues: (1) The independence of "Manchukuo" is an obvious fact and does not violate the Nine-Power Treaty. This is very clear in both theory and history. (2) Convening a conference of countries related to the Nine-Power Treaty in such a situation would only lead to empty talk and would not be beneficial, and would only worsen international sentiment. (3) Revising the Nine-Power Treaty, such as the inclusion of "Manchukuo," is a matter for the relevant countries to consider after recognizing "Manchukuo." (4) The adjustment of Far East issues must be conducted through Japan-US [Telegraph].)

Is Japan Preparing for War Against England? 28

Why Such Close Attention to Singapore?

(Tokyo) The British naval base in Singapore has an important relationship with the Japanese navy's maritime policy, and the naval authorities are paying close attention to it. Judging from the progress of the construction to date, it can be the most successful base after completion. (1) The construction of fortresses, the installation of gun emplacements, and the construction of barracks have been largely completed, and are scheduled to be completed by September 1935. If necessary, they can be completed at any time. (2) Large docks and auxiliary facilities have been built in what was originally forest and swamp land. The docks in front of the docks have also been completed and can accommodate the largest warships. The completion of the docks is also imminent in a few months, and only ground work will remain. The initial budget was 10 million pounds, but it was completed with only 6.9 million pounds. (3) The air base has a squadron of bombers and flying boats. It seems too few for the British Far East air base, but since air transport from the home country to Singapore can arrive in four days, there is no need for too many permanent aircraft. (4) In addition, there are flight squadrons organized by Europeans, Eurasians, Malays, and others in the Straits Settlements. (1st Electric Communication Telegram)

[P British Finances Stable]

Surplus of Thirty Million Pounds

(London) The British fiscal year ended today. After offsetting revenue and expenditure, there was a surplus of 31,144,000 pounds. The Ministry of Finance tonight wired this good news to Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain, who is currently fishing in the River Dee. When the budget was proposed last April, the estimated surplus was 1.3 million pounds and did not include provisions for paying the statutory sinking fund or repaying US debts. The total revenue for the past year was £724,567,000 and expenditure was £693,419,000, including the debt repayment sinking fund and war debt payments. Last year, the Chancellor of the Exchequer's expected revenue was £698,800,000 and expenditure was £697,500,000. In terms of revenue over the past year, income tax and surtax totaled £281,000,000, which is roughly in line with the budget. The largest increase in revenue was from property tax, which totaled £15 million, an increase of £10.05 million compared to the budget. Customs revenue was £286,000,000, also an increase of £17 million compared to the budget. Postal revenue was £13.1 million, exceeding the budget by £1.5 million. There was a special item of £10 million in miscellaneous revenue, which was the surplus from the war debt discount fund. In terms of expenditure over the past year, interest payments on national debt were reduced by £11 million compared to the budget. This amount was used to pay the unbudgeted credit payments to the United States of £3.25 million, and the remaining £7.75 million was paid into the debt repayment reserve. Today, the total amount of British floating debt is 1,450,000,000 pounds, including treasury bills of 799,000,000 pounds and temporary borrowings of 449,900,000 pounds, an increase of 34 million pounds compared to last year. However, the increase is due to the issuance of an exchange stabilization fund of 200 million pounds, which has considerable assets to offset. Therefore, after excluding the exchange stabilization fund, the amount of British floating debt today is 166,000,000 pounds less than on this day last year. (31st Reuters Telegram)

German Reparations to the United States 31

First Payment of Over Three Million Marks

(Washington) The US State Department and the German Ambassador today reached an agreement that Germany will pay 3,177,125 marks for the overdue 50,000 mark military occupation expenses and various reparations owed to the United States, in order to show good faith. This payment is due on April 3. (31st Reuters Telegram)

(Washington) This afternoon, Secretary of State Hull announced that Germany has now agreed to pay $1,250,000 in gold to cover the German installment payments to the United States due today. The total amount of this war debt is US$50 million. The German side has formally notified Hull that the payment will be made on April 3. Hull then informed the German Ambassador to the United States, Luther, that the US government cannot reduce or cancel war debts without the permission of Congress, and that there is no hope for a reduction or cancellation of war debts in the current Congress. Hull told reporters that the war debt due today is that stipulated in the 1930 war debt agreement, and its total amount is equal to all the interest on the installment payments of war debts, plus the German reparations to the United States for military expenses. Since President Hoover implemented the moratorium, Germany has not paid the interest and military expenses mentioned above. The total amount of German war debts to the United States today, calculated at the previous value of gold at US$20.67 per ounce, is US$724,186,141. Calculated at the current value of gold at US$35 per ounce, it is US$427,704,335. Hull further explained that since President Hoover again stipulated the exchange rate of the US currency at 59.06, the German war debts to the US automatically decreased to US$296,481,806, and the total amount of war debts owed to the US by various countries also decreased by approximately US$9,000,000,000. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau recently made a report on war debts, stating that Finland is the only European country that can pay war debts on time according to the treaty. In addition, countries such as France, Germany, Austria, Belgium, Hungary, Poland, Yugoslavia, and Estonia have already reserved funds, but have not paid a penny from July 1932 to January 4, 1934. (31st National Telegram)

US Fugitive Case May Cause Dispute Between Turkey and Greece 35

Greek Foreign Minister Hopes for Peaceful Resolution

Recent developments in the case of Mr. Insull, the American beauty from Constantine and former Chicago financial giant, threaten to create a dispute between Turkey and Greece. Turkish authorities, at the request of the US government, today ordered the arrest of Insull on a Greek ship. The ship has been detained in the Bosphorus Strait for forty-eight hours. However, Mr. Insull refuses to leave the ship, and the Greek shipowner has protested the detention to the Greek Consul in this area. Mr. Boop, Insull's lawyer, has been extremely active in Athens today, lodging a serious protest with the Greek Foreign Minister, pointing out that the Turkish government's detention of the Greek ship violates international law. It is expected that the Greek government will send a diplomatic note to Turkey regarding this matter. After receiving the Greek shipowner's protest forwarded by the Greek Consul in Constantine, Greek Foreign Minister General Maximos immediately telegraphed the Greek Minister in Ankara to question the Turkish government's reasons for detaining the ship. Mr. Boop has been receiving detailed reports in the past twenty-four hours, protesting to the Greek Foreign Minister that the Greek flag is not being respected at sea. He also telegraphed Turkish President Kemal, accusing Turkey of becoming a constable for the United States. Later, he sent separate telegrams to Turkish newspapers, urging them to jointly protest to the Turkish government. Mr. Boop received a telegram from the Greek shipowner, which read: "Turkish authorities allowed me to go ashore and instructed me to arrest Insull. I immediately protested to the Turkish government and reported to the Greek Consul." The Greek Foreign Minister recently informed Mr. Boop that he has taken appropriate steps and hopes that this matter can be resolved peacefully. Mr. Insull still hopes that the Greek flag will continue to provide him with protection. Relations between Turkey and Greece have been very cordial recently, but this matter may cause international difficulties. The Greek government feels very difficult, although it has made every effort to push Mr. Insull out of the country at the request of the United States, but the ship he is on is a Greek ship, which is virtually still within Greek territory. And the detainer of the ship is Turkey, with whom Greece has been striving for friendship for the past twelve years. Therefore, the Greek Foreign Ministry is thinking day and night, wanting to resolve this matter with a relaxed diplomatic approach, but public opinion in Athens is criticizing the Turkish government's detention of the Greek ship. (Reuters dispatch from Constantinople, 31st)

Gangs Rampant in Marseilles, Causing Shock Throughout France 39

Three Killed in Bloody Shootout in Tavern

Intricate Case Related to Previous Major Incident

Marseilles - At 1 AM today, four young men were sitting at a table in a Marseilles tavern when three men pushed open the door and entered. The four young men immediately drew guns and fired at the newcomers, killing two of them on the spot and accidentally killing a tavern customer. The four men then rushed out of the tavern. By the time the people in the tavern recovered from their shock and got up to chase them, the whereabouts of the murderers were unknown. One of the dead men had a loaded pistol in his pocket, with his hand already on it, but he was shot down before he could take it out. Only one of the three men was unharmed. According to him, he did not know who the murderers were. The residents of Marseilles were shocked by this tragedy. It is expected that this matter is related to the arrest of Feng Queer and Shi Piliito on March 29. Feng and others are accused of murder and robbery, as they are involved in the murder of Prosecutor Pu Lansi in February. They are currently being interrogated to clarify the suspected murder of Mr. Pu. These two men not only have power in the underworld in Marseilles, but also can influence the municipal government. Today's murder case is likely related to the arrest of Mr. Feng. The fact that gangs are rampant in the city of Marseilles has shocked the whole of France. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

Japan's Accelerating Seizure of Gold Mines in Jilin and Heilongjiang 64

--Investigation Shows Value of 4.7 Billion Yuan--

--Organizing a Large-Scale Mining Company--

Harbin News: The provinces of Jilin and Heilongjiang have always been the richest gold-producing areas in our country. In the early years, they were operated by the people of China and Russia, using completely placer mining methods. Due to outdated technology and lack of organization, there were no statistical figures for reference. The Japanese side is now actively engaged in development based on the survey results of Russian geologist Mr. Azolto and the South Manchuria Railway Co., Ltd., and is organizing the Manchuria Gold Mining Company, with a fixed capital of 12 million yuan. The pseudo-government authorities, the South Manchuria Railway Company, and the Oriental Development Company will purchase shares. The gold mine, which was originally richly endowed in China, will all be acquired by the Japanese. The details are as follows:

Gold Mines in the Li Hongzhang Era As early as when Li Hongzhang was the Minister of Beiyang in the Qing Dynasty, the Mohe River in the northernmost part of Heilongjiang Province was discovered to have gold mines. At that time, Russians gathered to reach thousands of people, and Chinese people gradually increased. During the eighth and ninth years of Guangxu, the Chinese and Russian population totaled more than 10,000. Within these two years, the area produced more than 219,000 taels of gold sand, worth more than 13.8 million yuan, which was extremely prosperous. At that time, as a result of negotiations between Li Hongzhang and the Russian government, the Russians in the area were driven out. In the fifteenth year of Guangxu, the Mohe Gold Factory was reorganized and run by the government. In recent years, it has gradually declined, with annual output of only a thousand taels or so.

Russian-Announced Ore Amount According to Mr. Aniertorto, a Russian geologist and trustee of the Harbin Office of the South Manchuria Railway, the total amount of gold ore buried in northern Manchuria is 94 million taels, with a value of 4.7 billion yuan. Mr. A is a geological expert, and the aforementioned amount of reserves is presumably estimated by comprehensively considering both theory and facts.

Investigation by the South Manchuria Railway According to the investigation by the South Manchuria Railway Co., Ltd., from 1926 to 1930, the amount of gold produced in Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces was as follows:

Jilin Province Heilongjiang Province

1926 47,800 2,184,600

1927 50,000 1,733,150

1928 50,000 1,282,500

1930 550,000 1,420,000

According to the left table, the amount of production in Jilin Province is small, but the actual amount may be several times this.

Surveying the Location of the Ore Bed There are also so-called mountain gold and rock gold, which are called ore beds. However, the ore bed area has not been carefully inspected. Because the source of placer gold ultimately belongs to mountain gold, it can be inferred that there must be gold mines in the upstream of the placer gold site. There has been no investigation in Jilin and Heilongjiang before. Japan is planning to investigate the distribution of placer gold and the state of mountain gold burial at the same time.

Data on Gold Production in Heilongjiang Province According to the "Mining Industry Records" published by Mr. Xie Zhongjiarong, the total amount of gold produced in Heilongjiang Province is estimated to be 500,000 taels per year. According to Mr. Dugasayev, a Russian, in October of the 16th year of the Republic of China, the estimated amount was as follows:

Aihui 135,000 taels Huma 48,000 taels

Mohe 9,000 taels Shiwei 19,000 taels

Nenjiang 2,000 taels Xiaoyuling 8,000 taels

Total 222,000 taels

According to this figure, it seems to be too exaggerated. The figures investigated by the South Manchuria Railway Company are listed below for reference:

Location 1928 1929 1930

Liyuan 1,000

Huma River 1,000 1,000

Fulahanchi Gan River 900

Wutong River 1,000

Hejin River 2,500

Total 25,650 8,000 28,400

According to the right table, there are significant changes in the amount of production each year. It is impossible to investigate whether this situation is related to the ore bed. The Japanese are studying it.

Gold-Producing Areas in Jilin The main gold-producing areas in Jilin Province are Ning'an, Muling, Yilan, Fangzheng, Mishan, and other counties in the northeast, as well as the vast gold-producing area in the southeastern part of the province bordering Fengtian. Among them, the Jiapigou owned by Han Dengju is well-known to Chinese and foreigners. In the early years, members of the Japanese Mining Industry Investigation Group came to the site for investigation and said that the gold mine was a rare ore vein in Manchuria. The factory has a clear width of about four feet and extends for more than 6,000 feet. There are three ore veins. No matter who, it is regarded as a promising gold mine. Based on this example, there are still a large number of gold veins similar to Jiapigou buried in various parts of Jilin. The amount of production in Jilin Province has always been collected by small-scale agricultural operations, and there is no way to collect statistics. The amount of gold production investigated by the South Manchuria Railway Company in Jilin Province is listed on the left:

Location 1928 1929 1930

Lingchuan 5,000 10,000

Yanhe 1,000 1,000 1,000

Total 1,000 6,000 11,000

(Northeast News Agency)

Japanese Military Actions in Shenyang 65

—Northeast People Suffer Cruel Treatment—

Shenyang Communication: When the Japanese army first occupied the Northeast, it first implemented its appeasement policy, claiming to be a friendly country. After the puppet organization was completed, it used it for its own purposes, and then acted arbitrarily and brutally. The following is a record of its recent actions in Shenyang:

Secret Agents Do Evil 66

The special service agencies, gendarmerie, and garrison of the Japanese army all hire Chinese traitors and those who are proficient in Japanese as secret agents. They go to various entertainment venues or private homes every day to secretly investigate whether there are any anti-pseudo and anti-Japanese behaviors. For example, if someone worked in a certain organization in the Northeast before the incident and is now unemployed, they are regarded as anti-Manchu and anti-Japanese elements. First, they extort money, and then they lead a team to arrest them, inflict extremely cruel punishments, and put them to death. The Japanese army also lets bandits run into various villages and let them harass them. Then, they order the pseudo-national military police to go to the villages to suppress the bandits. Rape, murder, arson, and fornication are everywhere. Wherever they pass, no one is spared.

Vagrant Harassment 67

Japanese vagrants collude with local bandits and hooligans to form fraud groups. They carry out large-scale fraud in cities and villages. Some even openly go to the villages to order the village chiefs to collect money from each household, or hide stolen goods to defraud farmers, or form gangs in cities to commit theft.

Rewarding Informants 68

The Japanese army not only secretly deployed a network of spies, but also bought over local ruffians and bullies as spies and rewarded informants. For each case reported, they are rewarded according to the size of the case, or paid a salary of five yuan, six yuan, or more than ten yuan per case. As a result, many unemployed and ignorant hooligans are bought and harmed each other. The poisonous plan is conceivable.

Conscription of Young Men 69

Recently, in the villages along the Anfeng-Shenhai line, the Japanese army has ordered each village to send several young men aged 18 to 24 (according to the number of households, each village has at least one and at most six). On the surface, they are given military training. In the future, they will return home after completing their studies and organize local militia. In fact, they have already been sent to the Jilin and Heilongjiang borders to undertake the transportation and construction work of the Japanese army. The farmers all know this situation and have to endure it under the threat of power.

Vicious Dogs Eat People 70

The Japanese police station raises a large number of police dogs in the affiliated areas along the South Manchuria Railway and trains them to bite people. Sunjia Station has the most dogs, about 400. Many livestock of the villagers were bitten to death. Many people in the vicinity do not dare to go to the station and call it the vicious dog circle. Every time the Japanese army captures our suspected people, they first torture them severely and then throw them into the dog circle to feed the dogs. The dogs compete for food, and the limbs are split apart. The tragic situation is unbearable to see. (Northeast News Agency)

The Pseudo-Legislature President Zhao Xinbo Suddenly Turns Passive 71

——Repeatedly Struck, His Spirits Are Low——

——Publicly Shows Passivity, Secretly Forms Factions——

Changchun Dispatch: Zhao Xinbo, the President of the pseudo-National Legislature, had already colluded with the Japanese before the Northeast fell, seeking foreign aid to develop his great desire for promotion and wealth. At the beginning of the puppet Puyi's usurpation, he again engaged in major activities, plotting to fill a certain important ministerial position in order to manipulate the pseudo-national government. This greatly displeased the Japanese side. As a result, he only obtained the position of president of the legislature, which was a great disappointment. Like Yan Jin and Zheng Xiaoxu, who flattered the Japanese daily, and Xi Qia, who acted in concert, he also tried to seize the opportunity to act, but he stopped because he did not get the consent of the Japanese. Zhao tried to make moves several times, but was struck down each time. Therefore, he became disheartened, sighing all day long, exhaling smoke, regretting that his many years of hard work had not resulted in an opportunity to betray the country for personal gain. So, he publicly showed passivity and secretly formed factions, secretly contacting the leaders of the pseudo-army. What kind of attempts he is making is unknown, but it has been discovered by the Japanese, who are paying close attention to his actions. If there is a flaw, I am afraid that Zhao will die without a burial place. The end of a traitor is hateful and pitiful.

Page 9

Xinjiang Inspection Notes (2) Special Correspondent of This Newspaper Geng Ya L]

Departing North from the Capital 72

At 5:00 PM on the 11th, I left the capital to cross the river and took a train north from Pukou. The 7:00 PM express train had few people and spacious seats, somewhat similar to the Shanghai-Ping train, but not as new and clean. The train traveled for thirty-five minutes and arrived in Chuxian County, Anhui. I saw many people selling bamboo baskets, hand baskets, and live chickens, and each vendor had lanterns, illuminating the area like daytime. Mr. Zhang Dechong from Chu boarded the train and talked about the provincial No. 8 middle school in the city, with more than 500 students. The facilities are also relatively complete, but girls are not allowed to study together. There are no girls' middle schools in neighboring counties, so very few female primary school graduates have the opportunity to receive secondary education. This is probably the same educational style in Jiangbei. Mr. Zhang is now the director of the Quanxiao County official factory office. He also said that there are many barren mountains and wasteland in Anhui Province. In Quanxiao County alone, there are as many as 80,000 mu, accounting for about three-tenths of the cultivated land. Half of it has now been reclaimed. The selling price per mu is no more than twenty yuan, and the official factory office is still making a large profit.

At 5:00 AM the next morning, drizzling rain fell. The train arrived at Tongshan (that is, Xuzhou). The city is located at the intersection of the Jinpu and Longhai Railways, connecting the four provinces of Jiangsu, Shandong, Anhui, and Henan. Commerce has always been developed. Last year, due to the impact of the recession, many banks and businesses went bankrupt. It has been a long time, and there is still no sign of recovery in the market. From here to the north, copper coins are only used in "large denominations" (that is, those worth twenty wen). If there are small denominations worth ten, you must exchange them out when you leave here. It is calculated that every eight small denominations can get five large denominations. Silver coins or corner notes from different provinces are not used in the north. If you are going to the Northwest, if you do not take the road through Suining, you should transfer to a train westward here.

In Tengxian County, Shandong Province, vendors sell full baskets of yellow pears, which are cheap and easy to carry, but the quality is rough and the taste is bland, good to look at but not to eat. Looking out the window as the train travels, the rain stops and the clouds clear. The ten thousand acres of wheat fields have leaves and seedlings that are two or three inches long, neatly arranged, interspersed with yellow soil, just like a large floral cloth with "yellow ground and green stripes." Northerners plant wheat in rows, which is not comparable to the random sowing in the South. Next to the fields, there are many willow branches with subtle spring intentions hanging down, and there are small birds on them, flying like shuttles. Every time the train stops abruptly, you can leisurely hear their chirping, as if they are declaring their freedom and joy. The ancients said, "Nature lends me its writings," and it is not wrong.

The rivers in Shandong Province are flooded during the rainy season and completely dry during the dry season, turning into roads. Water conservancy is rarely seen. Large rivers like the Yellow River sell a lot but have little profit. Governing them in ancient and modern times has not yet found a good method that works once and for all. Therefore, the irrigation of fields mostly relies on well water, which is drawn by human or animal power, which is twice the effort for half the result. There are many wells, and the wellheads are built with stones and poles, which also take up a lot of space. In addition, the cultivated land is mixed with graves, with mounds of earth like hills, and attached with land god monuments, all of which are enough to gradually reduce the cultivated land. It is requested that graves be buried in the fields. After several years, after being eroded by wind and rain, they can become large and small, and small can become flat ground, but it still takes a long time, and the stone tablets still stand tall, which is indeed impossible to improve.

At 11:45, I arrived in Yanzhou. The station is built as a "Jinpu Garden," with ponds and mountains, but lacks forest scenery. The city walls of the county seat are dilapidated, but very high, and the roofs of the buildings inside the city cannot be seen. Qufu has the Confucius Forest, the Zhougong Temple, the Sacred Temple, the Yanzi Temple, the Qisheng Wang Tomb, and the Zhou Lu Pan Pool, all famous scenic spots, which are far from the station, and I saw nothing. Only towering black mountains stretch endlessly, moving and getting higher, to show that Mount Tai is approaching. No one arrived at Taian. Many people scrambled to see Mount Tai. A villager forgot about the glass transparency, wanting to stick his head out of the window, and a piece of glass shattered with a bang, both shocked and ashamed, and his forehead was bleeding. I took out the medicine cabinet to apply medicine to the wound, and others persuaded him to move to another car to avoid compensation. Mount Tai is the first of the Five Mountains in China, towering hundreds of miles, overlooking the mountains. In the middle are the Jade Emperor Pavilion, the Wangmu Pool, the Guanshu Waterfall Pavilion, the Zhangren Peak, the Riguang Peak, and the Qin Emperor's Wordless Stele, etc. It is truly a great sight within the characters. The villager "looked up to the high mountains" and bumped his head and bled, which was not without reason. I remember going north last spring, just when the Great Wall War was breaking out. The anti-Japanese slogans seen along the way were more and more numerous the further north I went, and more and more intense. Now, it is just the opposite. In front of Taian Station, Ma Hongkui built a new "Monument to the Martyrs of the 15th Route Army for Suppressing the Rebellion" in memory of the Battle of the 19th Year, and a "Memorial Pavilion" on the mountain that issued orders. It should be covered with slogans. I did not know the true face of Mount Lu. Now, I pass by it again and only now know that it is this. Also, the city walls that I saw last year, which were covered with various slogans, have been newly painted with large characters of Jintan and other advertisements, which are once again shining brightly, making me feel particularly glaring.

From here to each station, more and more people boarded the train, and most of them were farmers, going to Tianjin and Luan to visit relatives, but in fact they still wanted to sneak into the Northeast to make a living. I once asked a villager who had just boarded the train, "The mountains in Shandong are bare. Why don't you plant trees?" He said, "The mountains are not suitable for trees. They don't grow even if you plant them." The train arrived at Gushan. The mountains on the east side of the road are mixed with soil and rocks, and are full of cypresses that are only three or four feet tall, dripping with green. The villagers also caught a glimpse of them, and looked at each other in silence.

At dusk, I arrived in Jinan. Those boarding the train should wait outside the railing first to let those getting off come out slowly. Unexpectedly, when the railing door was opened, they rushed in, even tripping five or six women and children. The Chinese people's disregard for social order can be seen everywhere. Jinan City is at the intersection of the Jiaoji and Jinpu Railways. Industry, commerce, and education are all quite developed. The famous scenic spots are Qianfo Mountain, Daming Lake, and Baotu Spring. The others are Shun Jing, Qin Shubao's Former Residence, and the Provincial Library. When I was young, I read the lesson "Three Famous Jinan Attractions" in Chinese class. The teacher said that Qianfo Mountain was named because it has a thousand stone Buddhas. I traveled to Lishan (that is, Qianfo Mountain) in the past, and there was no such thing. This is just guessing the meaning of the name. Or it is said that "Qianfo" is the mispronunciation of the two characters "Xianfu." Every household in the city has spring water, and every household has weeping willows. Daming Lake is the confluence of the seventy-two springs, and the scenery is picturesque. Baotu Spring is the giant of the seventy-two springs. Spring water gushes from the bottom of the pool, bubbling and making a sound, turning out of the water surface, about two feet high. In the past, there were only three strands, but now artificial excavation has added six strands. Algae, moss, shrimp, and fish each have their own secluded charm, which is truly beyond description. The saying "Hearing is not as good as seeing with your own eyes" applies to these places.

Last night, the wind roared wildly, and I felt something touching the car window, making a slight sound like broken jade. When I woke up from a dream, in the faint morning light, I suddenly saw lights like electric torches in the distance, shining with ten thousand points, like exquisite and transparent crystal. The branches of the cypress trees were still covered with residual snow, looking like cotton. Those falling on the stone steps and rails were also piled up and had not melted. I looked closely at the station sign and knew that I had arrived in Tianjin. Because I wanted to contact the Changtu Bus Company in Tianjin to negotiate remittance matters, and the Shanghai-Ping train ticket I was holding was delayed in Beijing, and it had expired here, I got off the train and stayed at the Nan Kai Shuo You Lou.

A Glimpse of Xinjiang's Export Surplus 73

Tianjin is the capital of Hebei Province and also one of the four major trading ports in China. Politically and economically, it is the center of North China. The Xin Sui Changtu Bus Company was founded in the winter of 1932. Although the main station is in Suiyuan, due to business and economic reasons, it has set up a head office in Tianjin. Mr. Zhu Xiting, the general manager, has a long-term vision and is well-planned. The initial capital was only 300,000 yuan, which has now been increased to one million yuan. I was introduced by three gentlemen, Gong Bicheng, Wang Luzhou, and Huang Jingwan, to visit and report the following information:

Xinjiang is isolated outside the border, and transportation is obstructed, making travel difficult, resulting in hidden resources that cannot be developed, and therefore culture and commerce are negatively affected. Therefore, the Xin Sui Changtu Bus Company was specially established to make travel to the border faster and to allow economic and cultural flow more easily. The company's capital was initially 300,000 yuan, and now it has been increased to 1 million yuan. The main station is located in the provincial capital of Suiyuan, and branch stations are located in Ulan Aili Gen, Hami, Guchengzi, and Dihua. The entire line is 5,980 li long (2,917 kilometers), with a total of 72 large and small stations. In addition to the main and branch stations, there are 8 rest stations and 12 gas stations. Regarding the support of Northwest cultural undertakings: (1) The company is willing to contribute one-tenth of its annual profit as a Northwest education fund, which will be used exclusively to subsidize Northwest students studying in the interior, regardless of ethnicity, and with equal treatment. However, recently it is only temporarily applicable to students from Xinjiang. When the fund increases, it will be extended to students from Qinghai, Gansu, Ningxia, Suiyuan, and Inner Mongolia. (2) The company offers special low prices for transporting cultural items to Xinjiang, such as school books and newspapers. (3) Students from the new province coming to the interior to study receive half price on the bus, and the poor are completely free. (4) Those hired to go to Xinjiang to run education are also exempt from bus fare. It is expected that this road will be the first shortcut for the interior to enter Xinjiang. If there is no obstacle from war, the business can be developed day by day in the only necessary traffic sense. However, the company has no monopoly idea. In the future, after a certain period of time, the government's strength can take care of this and can make the company without any sacrifice situation, the whole road is nationalized, its scale is expanded, and its management is improved. The effects achieved will be even greater. This is what we look forward to. Later, I discussed with them the remittance methods for this trip, and they enthusiastically supported and resolved the good method, which was very gratifying. They also introduced the person in charge of statistics of the company to tell the main amount of import and export of Xinjiang in recent years. A brief record is as follows:

A. The main products of Xinjiang, the amount of annual transportation to Suiyuan and export to Tianjin, are 3 million sheep intestines, with a total price of 2.4 million yuan; 150,000 pieces of lambskin, 750,000 yuan; 64,000 pieces of Kuqa black lambskin, 224,000 yuan; 20,000 pieces of Gucheng black lambskin, 26,000 yuan; 450,000 pieces of oily otter skin, 400,500 yuan; 30,000 fox skins, 270,000 yuan; 4,000 wolf skins, 48,000 yuan; 300 sable skins, 13,500 yuan; 700 snow sweep skins, 28,000 yuan; 30,000 gray squirrel skins, 24,000 yuan; 1,200 lynx skins, 21,600 yuan; 25,000 wild cat skins, 37,500 yuan; 3,000 wild monkey skins, 1,500 yuan; 22,000 pairs of fox legs, 17,600 yuan; 4,000 catties of deer antler, 80,000 yuan; 450 catties of antelope horn, 270,000 yuan. A total of 16 kinds, with a total price of 4.6167 million yuan. The above items are based on the investigation of the camel transportation era. In the future, when cars pass, they can all be suitable for transportation, and the amount can be increased sharply.

B. In addition, the main products of Xinjiang are still exported from the A route, and there are still only camel transportable ones, which are 120,000 catties of horse mane and horse tail, with a total price of 84,000 yuan; 45,000 pieces of Baha white lambskin, 40,500 yuan; 30,000 pieces of Kuqa white lambskin, 24,000 yuan; 22,000 pieces of Gucheng white lambskin, 19,200 yuan; 64,000 pieces of Kazakh red lambskin, 25,600 yuan; 2,500 pieces of blue sheepskin, 2,500 yuan; 14,000 pieces of goat board skin, 4,200 yuan; 3,000 pieces of dog skin, 5,100 yuan; 250,000 catties of camel hair, 125,000 yuan; 220,000 catties of American grain cotton, 36,000 yuan; 820,000 catties of white wool, 16,400 yuan; 1.15 million catties of miscellaneous wool, 172,500 yuan; 4,000 catties of dried deer antler, 2,000 yuan; 180,000 catties of raisins, 54,000 yuan; 65 million fritillaria bulbs, 13,000 yuan; 13,000 catties of wolfberry, 4,200 yuan; 20,000 catties of mushrooms, 18,000 yuan; 24,000 pieces of white fortunate sheepskin, 36,000 yuan. A total of 18 kinds, with a total price of 682,200 yuan.

The number of main products exported from Xinjiang in the above two items, A and B, is based on the survey during the worst period of the market in 19, 20, 21, and 3 years. It is found that the export amount of fritillaria bulbs, wolfberry, and mushrooms in the two most prosperous periods of 16 and 17 years would exceed more than ten times the current amount. Others such as fur, cotton, raisins, etc., the amount of exports to the Suiyuan area each year has decreased by more than 80% compared to the past. Its economic panic and price drop everywhere every year, the stagnation of exports, is indeed not without influence, but its main reason is that since the completion of the Soviet Union's Tuxi Railway, it has surrounded Xinjiang for thousands of miles, bordering my border everywhere, and transportation is extremely convenient. Therefore, for Xinjiang, it is not only regarded as the only market for finished products, but also recognized as a sufficient supply of raw materials. Year after year, various economic aggression attempts are carried out without any effort, and it is worth it that the internal disorder in the new province is frequent, and the eastern transportation is cut off, giving it an excellent opportunity. Therefore, at this moment, the export of raw material products and the import of finished products in the new province have been completely manipulated by the Soviet Union. It is a pity that if the Chinese people do not cooperate and catch up quickly, so that the northwest traffic will become more and more developed, so as to recover the rights that have been lost, then the future is hidden, and the square is booming.

The main prices of goods transported from Tianjin and Suiyuan to Xinjiang each year are 760,000 yuan for cigarettes, 68,800 yuan for high-quality wool, 35,750 yuan for medium-quality wool, 126,000 yuan for ordinary silk, 97,600 yuan for second-class silk, 285,200 yuan for linen silk piece, 93,000 yuan for cotton velvet, 31,600 yuan for medium-sized western medicine, 28,080 yuan for domestic pills and powder, 3,000 yuan for ordinary stationery, 6,800 yuan for leather finished products, 99,000 yuan for shoes, hats and clothing, 14,100 yuan for medium-sized cosmetics, 60,000 yuan for books and printed products, 10,400 yuan for wool yarn and finished products, 4,800 yuan for silk velvet and finished products (the above can be applied to car transport), 460,000 yuan for rice heart tea, 200,800 yuan for black tea, 195,000 yuan for San Jiu Da tea, 3,200 yuan for Longjing fragrant tea, 2,652 yuan for Pu'er tea, 6,720 yuan for Han smoke, 42,000 yuan for second-class cigarettes, 12,000 yuan for blue market cloth, 27,500 yuan for coarse and fine medicinal materials, 7,800 yuan for second-class pills and powder, 21,350 yuan for second-class western medicine, 14,250 yuan for second-class cosmetics, 1,200 yuan for inks and paints, 2,160 yuan for hardware, 4,100 yuan for seafood, 3,200 yuan for fine paper, 1,560 yuan for domestic fine porcelain, 4,500 yuan for domestic pens and inks, 2,240 yuan for domestic decorations. The total price of imports by the new province from the Xin Sui Road each year in the past three years averaged 2,726,562 yuan. Compared with the annual total export amount of 5,244,900 yuan at the same time on the same road, the annual export surplus is 2,518,338 yuan.

Xinjiang is rich in products, and the above surplus figures can already be seen. In the past, before the construction of the Tuxi Railway, the figures should be even greater. Since the construction of the road was successful, the above imported goods, except for cigarettes, tea, wool, silk, books, and Chinese medicine, are not much different from the past, and other goods have been greatly crowded out by Russian goods, and are declining day by day, even more than 70%. In addition, such as kerosene, gasoline, candles, matches, sugar, steel, hardware, cotton cloth, plain cloth, porcelain, glass, etc., the amount of large goods with a locked amount of several million yuan per year has now been completely replaced by Russian goods. From this, the great economic power of the Soviet Union in the new field can be seen, but it is all due to the convenience of transportation.

Sichuan Bandits Will Flee to Shaanxi and Hubei 74

Chengdu Dispatch: The five-route army of bandits continued to launch a general offensive on all fronts on March 22. There have been fierce battles in recent days. The Zhou Brigade of the Fan Shaoxeng Department on the left wing attacked the Banmiao area of Wangjiaping and the Wangjingshan bandit positions, repeatedly breaking through five layers of bandit fortifications. The Liao and Fan brigades and the Zeng and Xu regiments have made varying progress of thirty to fifty li after fierce battles in recent days. In these few days, Fan's division suffered more than ten casualties of battalion, company, and platoon leaders, and more than seven hundred soldiers, which was an unprecedented fierce battle since the bandit suppression by the division. About two thousand eight or nine hundred bandits died, leaving hundreds of corpses. Fan's division also captured more than three hundred bandit guns. On the morning of the 26th, after several fierce battles, the government troops made progress again and again, and recaptured Xijiguan Mountain, Exiangjing, Hongyan, Chenghuangmiao, and other places. That night, there was a strong wind and rain. The bandits took the opportunity to counterattack the new positions of the five-route army. Liu Xiang ordered the first and second routes to attack Changchi from both sides. This place is the gateway to Nanjiang and the location of the bandit's arsenal. Therefore, to take Nanjiang, we must first get this place, and then we can have no worries. After the four-route Yang army captured Jiangkou, the bandits on the opposite side are now retreating to Zhanggongqiao. The bandits in Wanyuan, because of excessive oppression of the people, the people could not bear their abuse, and secretly formed a broadsword team of more than a thousand people. On the 23rd, after a night of fierce fighting, the bandits could not support it, were driven out of the city, and retreated to the back of the mountain five miles outside the city. They are still confronting each other.

After the Sichuan bandits were recaptured by the government troops in Bazhong, their momentum became more and more constrained. Chiang Kai-shek Sends Personnel to Inspect Post-Suppression Work in Bandit Areas 76

Divided into over Twenty Items Such as Self-Defense Roads

Nanchang Correspondence: Chiang Kai-shek, considering the successive recovery of bandit areas in various provinces and the importance of post-suppression work and rural revitalization, has specially dispatched a group of senior officers from the Executive Headquarters to Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Hunan, Jiangxi, Fujian, Zhejiang, Sichuan, and Shaanxi provinces to coordinate with the respective provincial governments in organizing county-level inspection teams for post-suppression affairs. These teams will successively go to each administrative region and county to inspect and guide matters such as post-suppression efforts, the baojia system, self-defense, blockhouses, roads, disaster relief, etc. Herewith is a list of the post-suppression work and inspection items that the Executive Headquarters has ordered each county to undertake: (1) The organizational work of the people's training committees in each management area within the garrison area. (2) The organizational work of the post-suppression committees in each county. (3) The organization of the security teams in each county, as well as their quality, discipline, funding, defense arrangements, anti-bandit operations, and achievements. (4) The organization and personnel selection of the baojia system in each county, funding regulations, and the clearing, spot-checking, changes, and registration of household registration, and mutual guarantee by five households. (5) The organization of anti-communist volunteer teams or strong-arm squads in each county, as well as the number of teams, personnel, weapons, the abilities and training of the squad leaders, anti-bandit arrangements, and achievements. (6) The location, structure, materials, style, capacity, required funding and its sources, and guarding situation of the blockhouses in each county. (7) The equipment of roads, telephone networks, courier posts in each county, and the organization of nearby residents, as well as the guarding situation of fortifications and bridges. (8) The blockade situation in each county. (9) An overview of the joint military-political bandit suppression efforts in each county and the range of expansion and contraction of bandit-infested areas. (10) The disaster situation in each county, the amount of disaster relief funds disbursed and the methods of distribution by the emergency relief and temporary shelters, the number of people receiving relief, the situation of those left behind, and whether there are any remissions of land taxes. (11) The methods of disaster relief in counties where rear-area disaster relief shelters are located, the amount of funds received, the number of disaster victims sheltered, and the situation of review and training work. (12) The use of cooperative preparatory organizations in counties carrying out rural relief, the methods and amounts of loans. (13) The methods for supplementing draft cattle, agricultural implements, and grain seeds in areas where they are lacking. (14) The organization and lending methods of cooperatives in each county. (15) The reorganization of local finances in each county (the organization of budget and final accounts finance committees), the elimination of excessive levies and miscellaneous taxes, and all malpractices. (16) The handling of rural land in each county, the organization of rural restoration committees at all levels, the resolution of land and tenancy issues, and the methods of rural savings, loans, and supervision. (18) The situation of each county in carrying out public education, increasing the number of public schools, and literacy campaigns. (19) The achievements of administrative personnel and local gentry at all levels in each county in carrying out post-suppression affairs. (20) Other specially ordered inspection items. (March 27th)

Songjiang 77

Detailed Record of a Suicide Case Involving a Shooting of a Beloved Concubine

Recently, incidents of tragedies arising from love affairs have been frequently reported. Last night (31st) at around twelve o'clock, a tragic case of shooting a newly acquired concubine and suicide occurred involving Shi Shouhai, also known as Jinguan, the son of Shi Zhirui, the manager of the Songjiang Salt Office. The incident shocked the neighborhood, and onlookers blocked the streets. Shi Shouhai, aged twenty-one, came from a wealthy family in Jiantingshan, enjoying a life of luxury and indulgence. With a violent temper, he habitually carried a four-inch pistol, embodying the image of a pampered young master. Last year, he married a woman from the Xi family, who gave birth to a son this year, only three months old and still in swaddling clothes. Shouhai spent his days indulging in pleasure, frequenting brothels in Shanghai's Xiaohua Garden. He redeemed a prostitute named Baolian Laoqi for 5,600 yuan and brought her back on the 29th of last month, establishing a luxurious residence for her in Zhang Zhong's house south of Jiangjing Bridge in the city. Yesterday, he sent a fast letter to Shanghai, inviting two young ladies, Nie Qiaozhu and Liu Bin'yun, to Songjiang. He originally planned to accompany them to Hangzhou for sightseeing today. Last night, after returning home from watching a play, Laoqi slept on half of the bed in the upstairs room with Nie and Liu, heads together. Shouhai was working on writing at his desk. When Laoqi went to sleep, she had a slight argument with Shouhai. After finishing his writing, Shouhai undressed, intending to sleep in the outer厢樓 room. The carter, Zhang Jinting, suddenly heard a gunshot, followed by another in quick succession. Upon going upstairs to investigate, he found that Laoqi had already passed away, a bullet having entered through the left side of her nose. Shouhai was rolling around on the floor under the bed. He called for Zhang to help him up. Zhang and the two women were terrified and went downstairs to call for help. Then, Shi fired another shot, ending his life, lying sideways on the floor. One bullet was in the left side of his head, and another in his chest. The two female friends, in extreme panic, ran out naked and reported to the police officer on duty, who reported to the Public Security Bureau. Inspector Zhou of the Wu Patrol was the first to arrive at the scene for investigation. Three suicide notes were found in the overcoat that the deceased had taken off: one to his father, Shi Zhirui, vaguely expressing regret for redeeming a prostitute; one to his brother-in-law, entrusting him to take care of the family; and one to the prosecutor, stating that the incident was out of necessity and had nothing to do with others, requesting that it not be investigated further. This afternoon at two o'clock, Prosecutor Meng, upon receiving the report, rushed to the scene with Forensic Examiner Wang and bailiff Chen Rong for investigation. It was verified that the woman, Baolian Laoqi, had been shot, and three suicide notes were found, which her father confirmed to be her handwriting. The official ordered the town police to collect the body of the woman, Baolian Laoqi, and the gold necklace and heart-shaped pendant she wore were placed on file in the court. The female friends, Nie Qiaozhu and Liu Bin'yun, and the carter, Zhang Jinting, were taken to the Bureau and transferred to the Prosecutor's Office for investigation and handling. It was discovered that one bullet remained in the chamber of the pistol. According to reports, several days ago, Shouhai had demanded 6,000 yuan from the accounting office of the Songjiang Salt Office. The accounting office initially refused to pay, and Shouhai fired a shot, which penetrated the glass window. Upon seeing this, the accounting office opened the iron safe, took out a passbook, and withdrew 6,000 yuan to go to Shanghai to hire the prostitute. It is calculated that this pistol had fired four bullets, which is consistent with the one remaining in the chamber. However, the reasons for his death are varied, and no one is certain. Currently, the body of Shi Shouhai is being prepared for burial by his family today.

Qingpu 78

Jiangbei Bandit Yang Da Captured

Yang Da, a notorious bandit who had repeatedly committed major robbery cases in various counties of Jiangbei's Yancheng and Funing, was previously involved in organizing a robbery of the Changzhou Ban Junlong steamer last year and killing someone in prison. The Second District of the Waterborne Provincial Public Security Team had already apprehended accomplices Hua Kuailiu Mazi and Chen Xiao Erzi, recovering two firearms. All confessed that Yang Da was the leader. Approval was immediately obtained from the provincial authorities to execute them by firing squad. It has now come to light that Team Leader Li Xiaotang of the Second Team of the Waterborne Provincial Public Security Team stationed in Qingpu noticed that robbery cases have been occurring frequently in the eastern part of the county recently, with few arrests, and that the bandits involved often speak with a Jiangbei accent. He previously purchased a tracking line to apprehend them and, as a result, apprehended the notorious bandit Yang Da in Anzhuang, the second district. However, the criminal's testimony was cunning, denying any crimes in Qingpu. Therefore, Team Leader Li immediately transferred the criminal to the Second District Headquarters of the Provincial Public Security Team for further investigation.

Changshu 79

Tragedy Occurs During Play Performance

Recently, a Jiangbei opera troupe came to perform in Tianzhuang Town in the county. On the night of the 30th, dozens of villagers from nearby Hudian Township went to the performance intending to enter without paying for tickets, leading to a conflict between the two sides. After the performance, Zhou Lin, Qian Jinhe, and others dragged eight leaders of the opera troupe to West Street and beat them, also stabbing them in the neck, hands, and feet with bayonets. They then left. The eight were unconscious after being stabbed. People sent them to a trauma clinic and reported the incident to the local Public Security Bureau. The next day, the murderers Chen Yuanyuan, Chen Gaosheng, Jing Guansheng, Qian Jinhe, Zhou Lin, and others were arrested and sent to the county government for interrogation. According to their statements, they had prior grudges against the eight. They were immediately detained. The eight opera leaders have been sent to the Yuhe Hospital in the city, and their lives are in danger.

Wuxi 80

Wuxi Women's Circle Expresses Sympathy to Li Shuyun

Since the Liu Zhuomin case occurred, involving Li Shuyun, wife of Gu Renfa, the Commissioner of Civil Affairs of Jiangsu Province, and her mother, Liu, the arrest and escort for interrogation in Wuxi has caused a national sensation, attracting attention from all levels of society. The details have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. It has come to light that the women's circle in this county has unanimously expressed indignation at the arrest of Ms. Li and her mother, and has organized a delegation to express sympathy to Shuyun and voice support. Yesterday (1st) at 2:00 PM, delegation members Xu Jingxia, Sun Manshi, Guo Mohe, and 36 others gathered at the Education Association in the city and departed to the detention center to express sympathy, bringing biscuits, oranges, and other items as gifts. Upon arriving at the detention center, Warden Sun Gongwu declined the meeting and visit due to regulations. After repeated negotiations, they were finally allowed to enter. At that time, Li Shuyun and her mother were already waiting outside the cell gate. Upon seeing the delegation, they couldn't help but shed tears of emotion. The delegation presented the biscuits and other gifts, which Shuyun repeatedly declined, expressing gratitude and shame. The delegation then inquired about the details of the case. Shuyun said that she discovered Gu Renfa's bigamy one month before the Liu case occurred, so it was completely separate from the Liu case. Now, Renfa has consistently failed to provide concrete evidence, only resorting to evasive tactics. Now, she only asks the court to quickly summon Gu Renfa to appear in court for confrontation, so that the truth can be revealed. She also implored everyone to uphold justice and voice support, and requested them to telegraphically request Chairman Chen of Jiangsu Province to quickly order Gu Renfa to come to Wuxi for confrontation. While speaking, she sobbed uncontrollably. Her mother, Liu, also burst into tears beside her, moving those who heard. Afterwards, the delegation withdrew from the detention center, returned to the Education Association, and convened a meeting. All members attended, and Xu Jingxia was publicly elected as chairman and Sun Manshi as secretary. The proceedings followed due protocol. It was resolved that (1) the association would be named the Wuxi New Life Movement Women's Promotion Association Preparatory Committee Gu Li Shuyun Sympathy Delegation; (2) Xu Jingxia and Sun Wan were nominated to draft a telegram to request Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and Chairman Chen to quickly order Gu Renfa to come to Wuxi for confrontation to clarify the truth, and the telegram would be sent tomorrow (today); (3) Xu Jingxia, Sun Wan, Tang Lanyue, and Gu Yu were nominated to visit the detention center at least once every week to express sympathy. The meeting adjourned, and the preparatory meeting of the Wuxi New Life Movement Women's Promotion Association continued. Sun Manshi, Xu Jingxia, Lu Jingxia, Zhang Wenying, Tang Lanyue, Wu Shan, Guo Mohe, Chen Shouying, Gu Yu, and others were nominated as preparatory committee members. There were also several other important motions, which are omitted for brevity.

Water Police Cleverly Capture Four Robbers 81

The Ninth Team of the Second District of the Waterborne Provincial Public Security Team stationed in Wuxi received a confidential report the day before yesterday evening stating that several robbers, including Mei Zhenjun, who had robbed boats traveling between Suzhou and Wuxi were hiding in Chen Baitou Lane. Jiangyin Robber Executed by Firing Squad 82

Chen Sanlang, a bandit who burned and robbed Wang Xiaoda's family in Wangjiaba, the second district, was apprehended two years ago and detained in prison. Before a verdict was reached, Chen disrupted the peace and forcibly robbed Bao Dong Zhao Shouzhang of silver dollars in prison last month. The High Court dispatched Judge Wang Decheng of the Wujin Court to investigate and confirm the matter. After interrogation by the county, the case was reported to the provincial government, which issued a telegraphed order approving the death penalty. Yesterday (31st) at around 11:00 AM, Chen was taken to Lujiafen outside the North Gate for execution by firing squad.

Gaoyou Cargo Ship Capsizes, Shipowner Tragically Dies 83

Wu Lanzhou from Qingzhen Township in the Eleventh District of the county made a living by operating boats, specializing in transporting goods from Zhenjiang for merchants in the Lingyong Town in the area. The day before yesterday, the ship was loaded with four baskets of soybean oil (approximately 1000 lbs), approximately 5000 lbs of coal and iron, and other miscellaneous items from Zhenjiang. While sailing to the Shahu Kou area, it encountered a hurricane. Wu anchored the ship, but a raging wave crashed over the ship, causing it to sink. Wu and the others were submerged. A neighboring boat noticed and came to rescue them. Three people were rescued but were already barely alive. The three crew members recovered quickly, but shipowner Wu Lanzhou could not be saved and died immediately.

Tongnan Pingchao Kidnapping Case Solved 84

The home of Xu Mingyuan in the Pingchao District of Tongzhou was robbed by bandits. Before leaving, they kidnapped Xu's six-year-old grandson. The Third Battalion of the Provincial Security Infantry Regiment stationed in Tongzhou apprehended the key suspect in the case, Gu Chunsheng, and Xu Xinfa in the Yang residence on West Main Street in the city. Because the kidnapped child was being held in Shanghai, they were escorted there to search for him.
