Overview of Shanghai Shinyi Chemical Pharmaceutical Factory Co., Ltd. 213

Shanghai Shinyi Chemical Pharmaceutical Factory Co., Ltd. was initially founded by Dr. Xiafei, a German Doctor of Pharmacy. Since the 19th year of the Republic of China, under the advocacy of Mr. He Zikang and Mr. Bao Guochang, foreign shares were recovered and a fully Chinese-owned joint-stock company was established. The trademark was set as "Changming Brand" and re-registered with the Ministry of Industry. Thanks to the efforts of the two gentlemen, the internal organization was reorganized and expanded as much as possible. The products were excellent and the business flourished. By the 22nd year, it had successfully become a giant in China's new pharmaceutical industry. The progress and development in the 22nd year were particularly astonishing. If the situation is peaceful and the economy develops in the future, the future is immeasurable. Now, the overview of the factory is divided into equipment, manufacturing, and business departments, and the main points are described as follows:

Equipment 214

The factory's foundation was originally operated by German pharmaceutical manufacturing experts and was extremely complete. Over the years, it has been added to and enriched. In the past year, Mr. He and Mr. Bao have spared no effort to expand it. All kinds of chemical testing and manufacturing instruments and machinery have been purchased with the latest and most perfect equipment. Even at the expense of existing machinery with proven performance, for the sake of improving, they resolutely replaced them with the latest machines invented by pharmaceutical factories around the world. This is still the first application in our country. The two gentlemen are purely operating this new business with the spirit of scientific work. The innovation of medicine is the key to strengthening the nation. They do not focus on the meager profits of the present. To do a good job, one must first sharpen one's tools. This has been the case since ancient times. In today's world of rapid scientific advancement, how can we ignore the machinery that is the foundation of manufacturing? Therefore, the factory has everything it should have. It can be said to be second to none in our country. From raw materials to finished drugs, every medicine is made by machine and powered by electricity. Dr. Xiafei, the technician, is a world-renowned scholar. Based on his thirty years of research and experience, he is responsible for supervising the production of various products. As for other Chinese and Western experts, they can all use what they have learned and do their best. For the work of research and testing, they all explore based on the principles of pharmacology and physiology, and sacrifice a lot of money, time, and brainpower, regardless of the cost, in order to win the final reputation and success. Under the leadership of Mr. He, all employees of the factory can cooperate in division of labor. Even male and female workers are trained before starting work and are not allowed to operate rashly. They are supervised by technical personnel and adopt a purely scientific management method. Therefore, it is well-organized. Its complexity and refinement cannot be compared to any manufacturing work. The speed of its expansion is a model for the mechanical manufacturing industry. But its cost is also considerable.

Manufacturing 215

The perfection of the factory's equipment is as described above. But without talents to use its equipment, it is in vain. Therefore, the factory spares no expense to hire various specialized talents. Even for the animals used for testing, research, and raw material acquisition, a veterinarian is hired full-time, and a special veterinarian is required for temporary needs. The clinical research department, which experiments with new drug products, also has full-time specialist doctors from various departments under special contract. Its caution and rigor are so great. The rest can be inferred. If it is unavoidable to borrow talent from other countries, it is because there is a shortage of talent in our country, especially pharmaceutical technology talent. There are indeed knowledgeable and skilled people, but they are not enough to control. The country still has guest ministers. It should not be a problem for the factory and should be deeply understood. The factory's equipment and talent are equally difficult. It is appropriate that the products are excellent and can compete with imported products. All kinds of internal and external use, pills, tablets, powders, liquids, injections, etc. can be made by themselves. Among the products that have been made and praised and used by Chinese and Western doctors, the injection is just one item. There are already more than one hundred kinds. One-third of them were made in the past year. In addition to the famous Cibaoming, Vitamin Cibaoming pills, etc., the most famous new products, such as Vitamin Cibaoming injection, Fuvanein made from ovarian follicular internal secretion crystalline, Liver Lifter injection, powder and liquid made from liver crystalline, Healthy God Nourishing Blood Sugar Plasma, Labor Pain Inducer made from self-collected raw materials, Pituitary Cord Injection, Changming New Ga Injection chemically made, internal powder, etc. are unique in China. The most valuable of the factory's special products is Vitamin B crystalline preparation. The crystalline of Vitamin B is still the latest success in the world scientific community. The factory was able to extract Vitamin B from rice bran and silver skin in the winter of the 21st year and then successfully make the purest crystalline. Then, it is made into injections and tablets. Such a great success is not only the honor of the factory, but also enough for our country in the era of medical and pharmaceutical budding to raise its eyebrows in the world scientific community. There are many such excellent crystalline products in the factory. They are all new products in the past year and are not easy to come by.

Business 216

The factory's business has been developing since the 19th year and has been increasing year by year. The speed of its expansion is due to the booming industry and the needs of the environment. In the past year, due to the excellent performance of the products, the variety of products, and the tide of resisting foreign goods, the people of the country have patriotism. The medical community has all received the highest education and are excellent members of the intellectual class. The results of resisting foreign goods are easier to become consistent in fact. Therefore, in addition to this city, the factory has representatives residing in major cities in the country.

Bayer Pharmaceutical's World's First Suspended Electric Light Sign 217

Bayer Pharmaceutical recently suspended a great steel wire mesh between the two major chimneys of its Leverkusen plant and attached small blacks that moved sequentially like spider silk on it. Since this device appeared there, the general residents have been looking up at the sky in recent weeks, vying to look up and admire its magnificence and grandeur, which is beyond reach. According to the expert, these small blacks, like stars, are composed of hundreds of light bulbs. When the night falls, it emits light and shows Bayer's crisscross cross in the sky, shining brightly with great light. The circumference has a diameter of 230 feet, and each letter of Bayer's crisscross cross is 36 feet. Each side of this electric light sign has a Bayer's crisscross cross. However, because it is back-to-back, and one side of the light bulb is painted with aluminum paint to darken it, it can make both sides an absolutely clear electric light circle. Each crisscross cross uses 1,100 light bulbs, for a total of 2,200 bulbs. However, the actual current used is very small. The circumference of the two circles should be 720 feet. To facilitate climbing this electric light spider web, there is a bucket-style elevator. However, this is after the construction is completed. If it was built at first, then anyone who engaged in this project would have to climb the chimney, which is 415 feet high. According to the top of the two towering chimneys, there is at least a foot and a half of swing, and the diameter from the outer edge to the outer edge is 18 feet. How dangerous is it for those who work on it? However, the chimney craftsmen are all accustomed to this kind of movement and do not care at all, and proceed with their work calmly. This is also difficult and commendable. As for the net with electric lights, it is slowly raised and placed in its fixed position after the support cable is aligned. It is conceivable how difficult the project is to suspend such a great steel net in such a high altitude. Furthermore, because the net is extremely fine, it can be guaranteed not to be affected by the wind due to its excessive area. Therefore, even if it is suspended in the air, there is no danger of shaking.

Economic Publication Published on the First Day of the Week 16th Issue

Overview of Textile Import Trade in the 22nd Year 218

— Ye Zixiu

Import trade in the 22nd year showed a general downward trend, with the decrease in textiles being particularly significant.

Total Imports Textiles Other

21st Year 891 223 668

22nd Year 690 117 573

(Unit: Million Customs Gold Units)

The total of other goods decreased by only 14%, while textiles alone decreased by as much as 48%. In the 21st year, textiles accounted for about one-quarter of the total value of imported goods, which decreased to 17% in the 22nd year. Most textile goods are consumer goods for clothing. Under the circumstances of sluggish rural economy and years of international trade deficit, this situation can be considered somewhat satisfactory. The ups and downs of the main items are briefly analyzed below.

Cotton Cloth

Turning over the import trade statistics, the first thing one sees is cotton cloth. In the past few decades, the total import value of cotton cloth often ranged from 1.1 million to 2 million dan, with a value of tens of millions of taels, rightfully occupying the leading position. However, in recent years, it has decreased year by year, and the import value is no longer what it used to be. In the 21st year, imports were still more than 800,000 dan, worth more than 60 million Customs Gold Units; in the 22nd year, it further decreased to 30 million Customs Gold Units, and the estimated quantity must already be within 500,000 dan, only 20-30% of what it once was. Examining the Customs Trade Monthly Report item by item, the import volume in the 22nd year compared with the 21st year can almost be said to have decreased uniformly across dozens of items. The only exceptions are wide-width foreign yarn, floral prints, unlisted printed cloth, and striped poplin. Even these four items each have special reasons. Wide-width foreign yarn was originally mostly used as material for making handkerchiefs, and its value was particularly low. The import tax could not be levied ad valorem according to ordinary foreign yarn, and its ad valorem tax rate was relatively light due to the low original price, so import trade was concentrated on wide-width products. If we combine the calculation of both wide and narrow items, we can know that the import value has indeed decreased and not increased (the figures are roughly the same). Most of the floral prints imported were Russian goods. The quality of Russian goods is relatively thick, and the use is close to that of printed twill, unlike British and Japanese goods. The increase in the import of Russian floral prints in the 22nd year is in stark contrast to the sharp decline in Japanese printed twill. The increase in the import of striped poplin is due to the simple classification of the old tariff rules, where all dyed yarn products were subject to ad valorem tax, which was light, so striped poplin replaced bleached plain silk. As for the increase in unlisted printed cloth, it is due to the trickery of double-sided printed cloth. Ordinary double-sided printed cloth is only for sporadic decorative use, so the old tariff rules classified it as unlisted products and levied ad valorem tax. The ad valorem tax was reduced invisibly due to the impact of the decline in the original price, so ordinary printed cloth that originally did not need double-sided printing also deliberately made double-sided printing to take advantage of it, and unlisted printed cloth thus increased sharply. In summary, it can be seen that the so-called increase is the result of item transfer and is not enough to affect the general judgment of reduction. There are approximately two important reasons for the general decrease in cotton cloth. First, it is human nature that those with better living conditions first pay attention to clothing. Conversely, economic difficulties naturally lead to savings in clothing, abandoning high-end imported products and switching to cheaper domestic products. This is to be expected. Second, the domestic industry was originally more prosperous in cotton textile industry. Before the autonomy of tariffs, imported cotton yarn had already declined with the increase in domestic production. In recent years, tariffs have been repeatedly increased, and the import value of cotton cloth has decreased accordingly, which is quite natural. The current tariff rules are about half as high as the previous tariff rules, and they were implemented at the end of May of the 22nd year. The import volume of cotton cloth in the second half of the 22nd year was 8 million Customs Gold Units, which is about half less than in the first half of the year. Therefore, the future trend of cotton cloth import trade can be imagined. The import volume of cotton cloth since the founding of the Republic of China is listed on the left. (Unit: Dan)

Average from the 1st to the 4th Year 1,992,322

Average from the 5th to the 8th Year 1,631,514

Average from the 9th to the 12th Year 1,640,540

Average from the 13th to the 16th Year 1,642,082

17th Year 1,825,820

18th Year 1,805,325

19th Year 1,356,411

20th Year 894,113

21st Year 816,719

22nd Year 450,000 (Approx.)

Cotton

The import volume of cotton in the 22nd year was more than 1.99 million dan, which is much less than in the previous years. In the previous years, the import volume increased sharply to 3-4 million dan, which some considered an unusual situation. Now it has decreased sharply to 2 million dan, which may be considered a return to normal. However, in my opinion, the sharp increase in the import volume of cotton in the previous years was not unexpected, except for the hundreds of thousands of dan that were imported due to the extremely low price, which can be regarded as unusual. Today's sharp decline is an extraordinary state. Why do I say that? Because the supply and demand of cotton and yarn are mutually dependent, and the import of yarn and cloth is the import of cotton, but the form is different, and there is not much difference in substance. According to the import statistics of the most recent 20 years, although cotton was only hundreds of thousands of dan in the early years of the Republic of China, both yarn and cloth were around 2 million dan, and the direct and indirect import volume of foreign cotton was already in the range of 4-5 million dan. Since the European War, the import of cotton yarn has decreased sharply, so the import of cotton has gradually increased to 2 million dan. In recent years, cotton yarn has decreased from hundreds of thousands of dan to tens of thousands of dan, and cotton cloth has also decreased sharply by 1 million dan, so the import of cotton has increased sharply to about 4 million dan. The amount of indirect imports in disguised form has decreased, while direct imports have increased, and the total amount is often in the range of 4.5 million dan, so it is said that the sharp increase in the import of cotton in the previous years was not unexpected. As for the sharp increase in the import volume of cotton in the 22nd year, it is due to the accidental phenomenon of the increase in domestic cotton production, which is very similar to the situation during the European War. According to the estimate of the Yarn Factory Association, the average cotton production in China in the most recent 20 years is about 7.7 million dan. During the European War, it once increased sharply to 10 million dan. At that time, the direct and indirect import volume of foreign cotton also decreased to more than 2.8 million dan. In the 22nd year, the estimated domestic cotton production reached 9.7 million dan. At the same time, the direct import volume of cotton was about 2 million dan, and the indirect import volume and the import volume of the three eastern provinces were each tens of thousands, which should be similar to the number of 2.8 million dan. A good cotton harvest depends on the weather. How long can this accidental phenomenon last? It depends on the earnest work of the cotton industry authorities. Otherwise, the good times will not last long, and the import volume of cotton may not always be within 2 million dan in the future. The direct and indirect import volume of cotton in each year is listed on the left. (Unit: Thousand Dan)

Direct Import Disguised Indirect Import Total

Average from Year 1 to 4 234 4,943 5,167

Average from Year 5 to 8 284 3,671 3,955

Average from Year 9 to 12 1,439 2,967 4,406

Average from Year 13 to 16 2,047 2,247 4,294

22nd Year 1,994 500 (Approx.) 2,494 (Approx.)

Cotton Yarn

The import volume of cotton yarn has been small in recent years. In the 21st year, due to the relationship of discounted goods, the import of British fine yarn once increased, but in the 22nd year, it returned to the normal state of decline. The total import volume for the whole year was 27,700 dan, of which most were high-end fine yarns, except for the ordinary goods still exported to various ports in the southwest. Judging from the general trend of cotton yarn trade, imported goods are no longer important. The import volume in each year is shown in the table below. (Unit: Thousand Dan)

Average from the 1st to the 4th Year 2,595

Average from the 5th to the 8th Year 1,770

Average from the 9th to the 12th Year 1,126

Average from the 13th to the 16th Year 492

17th Year 295

19th Year 162

20th Year 46

21st Year 96

22nd Year 28

Hemp Goods

Imported hemp goods can be roughly divided into two categories: coarse and fine. Coarse hemp goods are mainly hemp bags made of jute. The annual import volume in China is about 1 million dan. In the 22nd year, imports were only tens of thousands of dan. There are two reasons for this. First, hemp is mostly used for packaging agricultural products, and the demand in the three eastern provinces is the largest, accounting for about 70% of the total. Now it is no longer included in this figure. Second, the import of rice, wheat, and other products has been considerable in recent years, reaching 40 million dan annually. These goods are mostly packaged in hemp bags. Counting 1% of the packaging weight, the annual import volume has reached 400,000 dan. No wonder the import volume of empty bags has plummeted. Fine hemp goods are mostly linen fabrics, most of which are used for embroidery, and a small part is used for Western clothing. In recent years, the export trade of embroidery products has been very prosperous, and Western clothing materials such as linen canvas and linen flannel are also active in the market. Therefore, the import volume of linen has increased from more than 2 million yards in the 21st year to more than 4.3 million yards in the 22nd year.

Wool Yarn

The total import value in the 22nd year was more than 53,000 dan, which is a very slight decrease compared to more than 54,000 dan in the 21st year. This is because the world wool prices were very cheap in the spring of the 22nd year, and domestic sales gradually shifted from undershirts to underwear and outerwear, and from winter to spring and autumn. In the past two years, the domestic production of domestic goods has increased day by day, and imported goods are also actively seeking local manufacturing. Although the domestic consumption may increase rapidly, the import volume may not necessarily increase sharply.

Woolen Fabrics 219

The total import value of woolen fabrics in the 22nd year was about 31,000 dan, which is a slight increase compared to 29,000 dan in the 21st year. The reasons can be attributed to both production and sales. In recent years, Japan's import of raw wool has increased sharply. Based on its special experience in mousseline, it is natural to engage in the export trade of plain woolen fabrics. As for the change in clothing, although ordinary robes and jackets have adopted less woolen fabrics in recent years due to the increase in tariffs and the low price of silk, the gradual transition of the entire form to semi-Western style is still in progress. The most obvious example is the popularity of outerwear in spring and autumn. Modern men and women each have one, and 80-90% of the materials used are imported woolen fabrics.

Artificial Silk

The import volume of artificial silk in the 22nd year was more than 69,000 dan, which is about 30% less than 100,000 dan in the previous year. This is the surface figure, but in fact, it has not decreased. Japanese artificial silk exports have always been mainly to China. According to Japanese export statistics, more than 25,000 dan were exported to mainland China in the 21st year of the Republic of China, and more than 2,700 dan were exported to the three eastern provinces. In the 22nd year, the quantity exported to mainland China by September was only more than 3,000 dan, but the quantity exported to the three eastern provinces increased sharply to more than 29,000 dan. Furthermore, the import volume of the three eastern provinces by November in the 20th year was more than 44,000 dan. There is absolutely no reason for the figure of the three eastern provinces to increase tenfold in one year. It is self-evident that there is a lot of smuggling and re-export. This is specifically for Japanese goods. If we include the number of Western goods smuggled from Hong Kong and other places, it can be concluded that the import volume of artificial silk has increased secretly while decreasing apparently.

Recent Situation of the Enamel Industry 220

— He Gongxing

The business volume of the Shanghai enamel industry in the 22nd year was a total of 4.27 million yuan in national currency; estimated:

Yiji Enamel Factory 1.1 million yuan

Huafeng Enamel Factory 950,000 yuan

Zhonghua Enamel Factory 750,000 yuan

Jiuxin Enamel Factory 460,000 yuan

Zhufeng Tongji Enamel Company 400,000 yuan

Shanghai Enamel Factory 340,000 yuan

Zhaofeng Enamel Factory 120,000 yuan

Other six small factories 150,000 yuan

Although the above amount is not as prosperous as in the 18th and 19th years of the Republic of China, it has increased by 20% compared with the 21st year of the Republic of China. In this autumn of rural bankruptcy and unrest in various provinces, this achievement is beyond initial expectations. However, this is only one area of production, (according to my country's enamel manufacturing factories, which are all in Shanghai) and the sales are to the whole country. The business income is only this number, and I am also not satisfied. One is that the sales lines have not been widespread over the years and have not penetrated into the people; the other is that farmers have a lack of understanding and still do not know how to use it, or even mistakenly believe that it is a noble product. In fact, after many observations, enamel utensils are most needed and most suitable for farmers. Not only are they durable and inexpensive, they are far better than bulky porcelain and bamboo and wooden utensils. Almost all kinds of enamel utensils meet the needs of the countryside, even if enamel round and square plates are used to dry flour, and large and small pots can also be used to store seeds, which cannot be invaded by tides and cannot be harmed by insects and rats. Asking about their value, they are all cheaper than bamboo and wooden utensils. However, among the farmers who can use enamel utensils now. There is not one in a hundred people. Therefore, if the enamel industry wants to develop in the future, it must first vigorously promote it to farmers. If this can be done, not to mention the annual turnover of more than 4 million yuan, even the daily turnover of more than 4 million yuan is not difficult.

The enamel industry is an emerging industry in our country. During the European War, it rose after the Japanese. In the past ten years, it has been catching up rapidly. So far, except for the area of ​​Northern Tianjin and Pingjin, where Japanese enamel products are still sold, Japanese enamel products in Southern China and the Yangtze River area have long been extinct. In the beginning, in order to jointly resist Japanese goods, all those who could cooperate with the industry did not unite in spirit and move forward bravely. Past facts are clearly verifiable, but each factory has different historical reasons, resulting in different interests. In addition, with the changes in personnel, suspicion arises. Since the joint business office of domestic enamel products was terminated for some reason last summer, the general public believed that the termination was a pity, given the difficulties in concluding the contract. However, if the form is separated but the spirit can be combined, it is like brothers dividing their families, and there is no harm. Therefore, since each factory has operated individually, they have all stated that they will maintain the turnover of the previous year, so as to achieve balanced development, neither infringing on others nor showing their weaknesses. And in their trade association. In order to prevent problems before they occur, we will further restrict the production of each factory, so as not to make their goods surplus, and then compete for outlets, leading to the bad habit of devaluation and competitive sales. Over the years, fortunately, everything has been safe. Starting from the 23rd year, we will further try to implement production control. The restriction of production in the previous year is only to revise the details: for the purchase of raw materials, we plan to jointly purchase them. Not only will the wholesale price be cheaper, but all kinds of raw materials used will also be standardized from now on.

The price of enamel products is uniform throughout the industry. Compared with previous years, the Shanghai market has been declining, and the rural economy of the provinces is on the verge of bankruptcy. In order to cater to the psychology of buyers, the industry has created secondary products in addition to genuine goods: it is cheaper than genuine goods, so it is convenient for ordinary people to purchase. Last year, the sales in the Nanyang area were fortunately for this secondary product. Not only did the sales increase greatly, but the Japanese goods were greatly robbed, because the prices were the same, and the quality of our goods was better than that of Japan, and no one asked about Japanese goods. Therefore, the sales of the enamel industry in the spring and summer of last year were the best in the Nanyang area. Fujian and Guangdong were also not bad. However, the Yangtze River area and Sichuan province were very deserted. Judging from the business situation over the years, during the summer and autumn, the Yangtze River gang was a trading area, and no one was not excited for a while, but last year it was so lonely, which was not expected by the factories at the beginning. After summer went away and autumn came, it was still immobile. At this time, the trading period of the South China gang had passed, the inventory of each factory was piling up, the business was stagnant, and the economy was panicked. In view of the effectiveness of price reduction in the past, I had no choice but to reduce the price again, which was named a special price category. First, the accumulated second-class goods and test products of each factory were included in the special price category for sale. With a publicity, buyers followed. However, the above-mentioned second-class goods and test products are limited, so how can they be popularized? Helplessly, buyers only seek cheap prices and do not care about the workmanship. If they do not continue to sell, no one will ask about genuine and secondary goods. They have no choice but to reluctantly treat the secondary goods as special goods to meet the sales. The turnover in September and October was about 2 million yuan, which is almost half of the annual turnover. Because of a slight price reduction, it was so popular that I don't know why. After investigation, it was found that the trafficking households had seen through the weakness and used it to coerce, which was no different from being used by them. Since January 28, the financial resources of the business community in various ports have been tight, which cannot be denied. All trafficking businesses are unwilling to wholesale goods. And in their warehouses, there is no shortage of storage, which can still be used for sale, and it is not too late to wholesale after the sale is completed. January 28 is almost two years ago, and the inventory of trafficking merchants in various ports is gradually sold out. I am worried that there is no way to meet the market, and I am about to wholesale from the Shanghai factory. Therefore, even if the enamel products at this time are not reduced in price again, there will be a large number of sales, but it may not be crowded in September and October. The enamel bottle industry, due to a temporary over-worry, unnecessarily sacrificed the price of goods and silver to about 400,000 yuan, which is also a small lesson learned by the industry in the 22nd year. However, in this era of advocating domestic goods, small profits and more sales are the right way; if you lose the east corner, it is not difficult to recover the mulberry elm.

Our country's enamel products were originally imitated from the East. For more than ten years, we have spared no effort to research and improve them, and we have long been better than the blue and on par with Europe and the United States. However, because sales are mostly in the upper and middle classes, we strive to improve the styles and patterns. Taking the washbasin as an example, there were only flat-edged and rolled-edged shapes at the beginning, but now we have advanced to make deep-shaped flared edges and other styles. The patterns used to be only blue flowers and ice flowers, but now, in addition to electro-optical printing, spraying, and more, we have advanced to make pile tea and gold trim styles. As for the color, the more it is made, the better it is, bright and dazzling, unprecedented　People in northern China have always liked to use copper washbasins, and each one costs 3-4 yuan, saying that although the value is high, there are more than ten taels of waste copper that can be sold for a price after it is damaged. Therefore, the copper workshops in the City God Temple area of ​​Shanghai can sell 40,000 copper basins to the north every year. Since the sale of deep-shaped enamel washbasins last year, the above-mentioned copper basins have been greatly affected, and many have changed from copper to enamel.

The Economy of Soviet Russia in 1933 221

— Yang Xianxu

The most noteworthy event for Soviet Russia last year was the further consolidation of its international standing. On the one hand, relations with Germany have progressed compared to before. On the other hand, France and various Eastern European countries successively concluded treaties of friendship with Soviet Russia. Furthermore, the United States' recognition of Soviet Russia in November was a significant event both economically and politically.

Last year, Soviet Russia still focused on improving its domestic economy and financial policies. While progress in industrial construction was steady, it devoted great effort to promoting all previously established enterprises. In industry, although the increase in production rate was only 16%, the overall production increase rate reached 22%. According to official figures, last year, the income of general industrial workers increased by 9.1%, while heavy industry saw an increase of 11.5%. Labor productivity in major industries increased by 10.2%, and production costs decreased by 1.5% to 2%. The reason for the increase in labor productivity is because a law was enacted in 1932 to severely crack down on unwarranted absenteeism by workers and employees. In other words, bread coupons were not issued to any staff who were absent from work without a valid reason.

Observing the entire industry, last year was indeed quite successful. However, some sectors failed to complete their planned production schedules. The steel industry only completed 78%, the forestry industry only 78.6%, the glass industry 71.6%, and the textile industry 95.4%. According to the Second Five-Year Plan, the output of major industries should increase by 21% this year, heavy industry by 23%, light industry by 10.6%, and the production of general consumer goods should increase by 16%.

Regarding the financial part of the 1933 fiscal year, the budget anticipated revenues of 35 billion rubles and expenditures of 32 billion rubles. In reality, revenue reached 39.2 billion rubles, and expenditures were 36 billion rubles. The business tax of state industrial and commercial organizations, which was originally the largest source of Soviet Russia's national revenue, exceeded the original estimate by 1.2 billion. Furthermore, an additional 2 billion rubles of income exceeded the planned sales of food and manufactured goods. There was also 600 million rubles from the sale of national bonds. The actual expenditure exceeded the budgeted expenditure by 1.5 billion rubles, which was used for the development of economic enterprises. Local budgets increased by 400 million, and the salaries of agricultural workers exceeded 200 million rubles. As for this year's (1934) budget, the anticipated revenue is 48,879,416,000 rubles, and the anticipated expenditure is 47,308,416,000 rubles, with 1,571,000,000 rubles as a reserve fund. As observed from the budget, economic enterprises increased from 24,865,900,000 to 33,345,700,000 rubles. Social and educational undertakings increased from 2,341,300,000 to 3,016,000,000 rubles. Administrative expenses increased from 2,400,500,000 to 2,889,800,000 rubles. The increase in military spending was not significant, rising from 1,416,600,000 to 1,665,000,000 rubles. However, we cannot draw any conclusions from this, as there is still a reserve of 11,360,850,000 rubles in the heavy industry sector. This could be allocated to increase military spending at any time.

Soviet Russia's international balance of payments improved last year compared to before. In the three years before 1933, international trade had been characterized by trade deficits. We can see this from the following (in units of 1,000 gold rubles):

1930　　　　　1931　　　　　1932

Exports　　　　1,036,371　　　811,210　　　563,844

Imports　　　　1,058,825　　　1,105,034　　　698,693

The complete statistics for 1933 have not yet been compiled. However, exports for the first nine months totaled 367,364,000 rubles, and imports totaled 274,285,000 rubles. This resulted in a trade surplus of 93,097,000 rubles. The trade deficit of previous years has now turned into a surplus. On the import side, various countries have reduced their exports. The UK's exports to Soviet Russia in the first nine months totaled only 24,988,000 rubles, while the same period in 1932 was 71,401,000 rubles. The decrease amounted to more than 46 million. Germany's exports decreased from 254,255,000 to 131,483,000 rubles.

According to Stalin's declaration, Soviet Russia's commercial debt abroad at one point reached 1.4 billion rubles. By 1933, this commercial debt had been reduced to just over 450 million rubles. Soviet Russia is also a gold-producing country, and it is estimated that its current annual output is over 100 million gold rubles.

Last year, Soviet Russia's agricultural development was surprisingly successful. Both the spring and winter harvests were excellent. The Soviet authorities consider this to be an unprecedented bumper harvest. According to the latest official statistics, the harvest of major agricultural products in 1930 was 83,540,000 tons, in 1931 it was 69,480,000 tons, in 1932 it was 69,870,000 tons, and in 1933 it was 89,800,000 tons. Before the European War, Soviet Russia's most abundant harvest was in 1913, which was 80,100,000 tons. Therefore, the harvests of 1931 and 1932 were both about 10 million tons less. The official claim is that the food consumed by the people is greater than before the European War, especially with the rapid increase in population, which has increased by 25 million since 1913. However, it is undeniable that the harvests of 1931 and 1932 were less than any year before the revolution in 1914. The production of barley in 1933 was 7.5 million tons more than in 1932, and wheat was 4 million tons more.

Soviet Russia's tax system has now been changed to in-kind taxation, which is of considerable benefit to the people. Furthermore, because the leading talents of Soviet Russia are all able to fulfill their duties and strive for improvement, it is no wonder that the country's progress is so rapid.

Distorted development...The golden age

Last week, from March 26th to 31st, the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange, happened to be the last day of early March, with settlement in between, and May was just making its debut. The trend was favorable, and the high market price did not diminish the strong appetite for more. New high prices emerged one after another, advancing steadily, with a momentum suggesting that the Salt Tax would not stop until it was below 70%. Commercial depression, with government bonds developing in such a distorted manner, reaching its peak, can be called the golden age. Whether the future will continue to develop, hover temporarily, or fall back immediately, is all possible. Speculators also have a dilemma of advancing and retreating. However, the majority of both long and short positions, big players, and those holding long positions have real strength, with short-term speculative profits in mind. There are also many major short sellers preparing to deliver, with longer-term speculative thoughts. Based on this speculation, unless the environment changes, the market price is unlikely to undergo major changes, with a greater component of hovering stability. We will wait until after the events of April to start the contention between long and short positions. The "Ninety-Six Affair" was short, quick, and has passed, but while the various bond markets are advancing rapidly, there is still a state of continuing struggle. Free Talk

The Fate of Poets 227

— Mu Mutian

Shortly after the suicide of the poet Zhu Xiang, I received news that the French "Poet King" Paul Fort was experiencing financial difficulties. This talented poet, who had published more than thirty collections of poetry, was not only ill but also poor in his late sixties, which was truly distressing.

"I am a tree of poetry," Paul Fort once said in his own poem. He had a unique talent for poetry. His prolific works had gained a wide readership. Perhaps it was due to the global economic crisis, or perhaps it was due to changing times, but the "Poet King" Paul Fort had fallen into such dire straits in his later years. If Paul Fort was like this, one can only imagine the situation of other poets.

Is this how the fate of poets should be? I can't help but ask. At the same time, I also think of the suicides of poets. Of course, we are not counting those who committed slow suicide and "homicide." Chatterton, G. de Nerval, Yssenine, Mayakovski, Kitamura Tokoku, Ikuta Shungetsu, Wang Guowei, and Zhu Xiang all died by suicide. In addition, many poets also lived in poverty for most of their lives. Why is the fate of poets so often like this?

Society wants people to sing their praises, but most poets have no flattering bones. Society wants people to join in their corruption, but most poets are upright and unyielding. In this way, they are bound to face their fate of "poverty."

Like the rabbit mourning the fox's death, I feel sorrow for my kind. I heard that the Japanese poet Horiguchi Daigaku recently published "A Selection of Paul Fort's Poetry" and plans to send the royalties to the original author. I wonder how much this international friendship will help Paul Fort economically?

From the poet Paul Fort, I also think of the novelist Dieko Bora Lai from the same country who traveled to China some time ago. A single book, "The Holy Virgin in the Sleeper Car," earned him an income of 2 million francs. It seems that making a fool of oneself and performing can lead to a good life!

Hope 228

— Wu Benxing

Year after year, wandering at the ends of the earth, but where is a glimmer of hope?

Could it be placed in the sky, stirred up by the fierce wind,

rising faintly, like the smoke from evening cooking fires,

drifting to the land of nowhere?

Could it be printed on ice,

melted by the scorching sun,

slowly, like the falling flowers of late spring,

drifting to be buried in the vast ocean?

Ah! I am seeking a glimmer of hope!

Year after year, wandering at the ends of the earth~

Small Hands 229

— Xu Ying

I saw my friend Shan on a asphalt road lined with graves on both sides.

"Hey," Shan greeted me first, "don't you recognize me?"

How could I not recognize him? Shan still looked the same, it was just his luxurious new clothes that made me a little hesitant. We shook hands, Shan's hand was warm, oily, and plump. The cuffs of his white shirt were snow-white.

"Aren't you working at XX?" I looked down at my dry, wrinkled, and rough palms.

"What work?" he smiled, "I haven't been 'working' for a long time. Now I'm practicing holding a baby, hahaha..."

He asked me to go to his house to see their little animal. As we walked, he talked about the little animal, making small talk with me. I was puzzled for a long time, and finally understood, "Oh, he's talking about his child!"

When we arrived at Shan's house, Qi was standing there wearing all black, holding a little baby covered in velvet. I was surprised, "What wind blew Qi here? What trick are this clever woman and Shan playing again! This woman is said to be at XX..."

Shan smiled, ran forward, took the baby, and said, "You don't even recognize Qi!" Then he turned his smiling face to Qi and said, "He didn't recognize me on the road either!"

The woman laughed like silver bells, swaying her slender waist.

"Look at our little animal, isn't it cute?" she said.

Oh, I understood, they were a couple.

The little animal had lively black eyes. When it saw a stranger, it cried. The couple hurriedly comforted the child, ignoring me. I stood aside, thinking that we used to be on the same line, I knew you, you knew me. Now you are on the line, I am off the line, how could I dare to presume?

"Your little animal is really good, really good, really good, really good!"

After saying a string of "really good," I made an excuse and left.

Concerning the Libelous Accusations of He Jiahuai (Continued) 230

— Xu Zhuanpeng

Next, let's talk about our article dispute. He says, "Zhuanpeng insists that I took his articles without his permission, I truly don't know what his intentions are?" But I say, except for the "Chariot of Water" piece, which I did receive permission for beforehand, all the others were without my permission. My fault is only that I didn't argue with him after he changed the name and published it. He says that my "Prison Break" was something that neither I nor my friends were satisfied with. I can say that there isn't a single thing I write that I am satisfied with, but this work that everyone is dissatisfied with, changed its name, added and subtracted about 300 words, and then published, became his proud "masterpiece." I ask, is there any completely terrible work that, after only modifying three hundred or so words, becomes a "masterpiece?"

Whenever I entrusted Jiahuai to recommend an article, he would always say, "This article is not well written!" At first, I didn't dare to have malicious suspicions, but now it seems that he said it was bad first to discourage me, and then he took it to publish, which he could then justify.

Before Shi Heng exposed this matter, Zhao Jiabi and Shi Heng mediated, wanting to resolve this matter secretly. However, Jiahuai denied it to Zhao, saying that some of his novels only took my idea. Later, he also said that my article had been revised by him, and he had revised it a lot. When I heard this, I just smiled and dismissed it, never imagining that he would have the gall to write it down.

Apart from my first one or two novels, where he added and revised more, the rest were merely changes in wording. These changes in wording were only to conceal the difference in writing style between the two of us. I have also opened a list below.

(1) Toothache: This was my first piece of work, originally very simple. He did indeed add a lot, but it was definitely not as he said, increasing it from two thousand words to six thousand words. My original draft was about three to four thousand words. However, everyone can find this piece and take a look; it is still a terrible mess.

(2) A Soldier's Wife: I originally sent this article to New Moon (Xin Yue), whose editor at that time was Mr. Shao Xunmei. After reading the manuscript, he said it was usable, but New Moon shelved it for two months without publishing it. I wrote a letter to ask for it back, and he replied that it was lost. At that time, Jiahuai was doing proofreading in the editorial department of New Moon Bookstore, so I asked him to check, and he replied that he couldn't find it. But after a summer vacation, I returned to Shanghai and saw it published in Literary Monthly (Wenyi Yuekan) under his name. Afterwards, when I met Jiahuai, I was afraid that Jiahuai would blush, so I didn't mention it. The original text was six to seven thousand words, and he stretched it to more than eight thousand words.

(3) The Sixth Child: He said, "I sent Zhuanpeng's original manuscript to Eastern (Dongfang) with my name on it." I originally entrusted him to recommend this manuscript to Eastern, but on my original manuscript, he changed it to his name the first time he sent it. I didn't know this secret beforehand, only after it was published did I see that Jiahuai's name had been changed. He also said he changed it, but this article didn't mention the extent of the changes or how many words were added. Citing the fact that he bothered the editor as proof that my original work was not good.

(4) Fishermen's Joy: He said he revised it three times, but I don't know how he revised it. According to my examination, he only piled up a little description. Adding about a thousand words is probably right.

(5) Chariot of Water: I had agreed to this article, because Modern returned his manuscript once in a row. He seemed resentful and told me, and at the same time, he discovered the newly written "Chariot of Water" in my drawer. After reading it, he insisted on taking it and complained to me about his own difficulty in writing. I agreed to him. I still have this original manuscript, and he only added a few hundred words.

(6) Valley Night: Some sentences have one or two words, or some lines have one and a half sentences that he changed, but he changed very little. This is a work that I myself consider slightly satisfactory. I was very happy to ask him to recommend it to Literary Monthly, but after a long wait, the published work changed its name again.

(7) Prison Break: When I finished writing this article, I happily sent it to him to read. After reading it, he shook his head and said it was not good. But later, it was published in Literature (Wenxue), and he called it his own satisfactory work in his article. He said, "Although I didn't notify him when I revised it, I wrote a letter to tell him before it was published." This is a fabrication. The words he added didn't even amount to a hundred.

(8) Gambling Den: He said he revised about three thousand words, but according to my investigation, it was less than six hundred words.

The other three articles—Blind Woman, Dinner, Entertainment—were not changed by a single word. He made some deletions and revisions to my articles, which I had already stated a month ago in my letter to the editor of Modern. I don't want to take the articles he revised as my own. If I take the articles back, I will still revise them according to my own writing style, in my own original way. Of course, I can tell which parts of my own articles he has revised.

Recently, many people in the press have said that I have received a share of the profits. Jiahuai also concealed this point in his confession. My article was taken by him and published under his name. He used the manuscript fees, and he still asks me what my intentions are?

Jiahuai said in his confession that he wants to embark on a solid path of "new life," which everyone would like to hear. But I hope that before his "new life," he washes himself several times, washing away all base and sinister behavior. Otherwise, like a monkey wearing human clothes, walking on the "new life" path, it is not a very glorious thing! (The End)

Editor's Note: Regarding the issue of creation between He and Xu, this publication has spent enough space. We intend to end it here. We will not publish any further submissions from either party.

Sketches of Beiping 231

— Yao Ke

(4) Random Strolls

What people in Beiping call "liuda liuda" (溜躂溜躂) is actually what is meant by taking a walk; the Shanghai term "dang malu" (蕩馬路) is similar. But sometimes the meaning of "liuda" seems to be more than just "dang malu" and also implies "baixiang" (白相, wandering around for pleasure), which can only be expressed by someone who is experienced in "liuda."

Strolling westward from Dongdan Archway to Dongchanganmen is a straight and spacious avenue—Dongchangan Street—which is much wider than Rue Edward VII in Shanghai. Along the north side of the street is a stretch of lush green trees, concealing hotels of varying heights, all of which are Western-style. Before dancing was prohibited, it was a place of bustling activity. The south side of the street is the parade ground of the garrisons of various countries, which stretches continuously. The outside is enclosed by wooden fences and barbed wire, prohibiting idlers from entering. The base of the parade ground is about a foot higher than Dongchangan Street, probably because it is constantly filled with soil and raised. Along the south side of the parade ground are the thick walls of embassies and military camps. The walls are full of honeycomb-like gun holes, which, it is said, were built after the Boxer Rebellion in 1900 to guard against the "rebellion" of the Chinese!

Strolling further west, passing through Dongchanganmen, is the front of the old imperial city. Two white stone dragon-carved ornamental columns stand on both sides, and the "Five Dragon Bridge" with five white stone carved railings lies across the open space. Beyond the bridge is the towering Tiananmen gate tower. The vermilion city walls, with five arched gates facing the Five Dragon Bridge, create a magnificent and solemn scene. However, upon closer inspection, the railings on the city tower have been eroded by wind and rain. If one were to climb the tower, it would surely be covered with thick dust and cobwebs! The vermilion-colored plaster on the city walls is also covered with a layer of dark gray, and the bricks are exposed where it has peeled off in patches. The carved railings of the Five Dragon Bridge also show a dilapidated appearance, with grass growing in the cracks of the stone slabs on the bridge surface. The two ornamental columns are protected by stone railings and are relatively the most complete, but the western one has a crack near the top!

Going north from the Tiananmen entrance is what is called the Forbidden City, while strolling south can take you all the way to Qianmen. But whether you go north or south, what unfolds before you is only a scene of decay. The things you see, even a broken stone slab under your feet, can tell you of its former greatness; but because you know its former greatness, you feel even more sorrow for its current decline. Indeed, everything in Beiping is in decline!

Strolling back along the original route, if it is at night, you will encounter several rickshaws that specialize in soliciting business around Dongdan Archway.

"Sir, let me take you for a liuda liuda around the east. There are good ones... Russian... Korean... newly arrived from Shanghai..."

And so you feel that even "liuda liuda" has declined.

On Translation (Continued) 232

— An

Three, the aim is to benefit people. Introducing culture and translating works is like doing business. But in addition to benefiting the academic and intellectual communities, there should be no other aims. Western scholarship is also vast and boundless, but if it is of no use to us, even if you are proficient in the original text and the translation is accurate, the effort is in vain. Therefore, one should first:

A: Establish a position. "Brother advocates political reform." Well then, good, you've established a position. If you want to do translation work, then translate famous works on politics, so that the work and the position are not too far apart. But it is not appropriate to translate "New Cooking Methods" because of so-and-so's personal request, or to translate "Research on Artificial Silk" because of so-and-so's company's employment. Because even if the translation is accurate, it is too much of a waste of effort. The terminology is different, the methods of expression are also different, it is difficult; it is a waste of one's own time and energy, like a thoroughbred horse carrying a pagoda car up the Taihang Mountains, which makes others feel sorry for it; moreover, it is possible that in the future one might translate "Research on the Treaty of Versailles" or "International Public Law," and have it placed next to things like "New Cooking Methods" in bookstores, which would also feel quite incongruous. I have heard that many students returning from abroad casually pick up novels and translate them, which shows that they have no position.

B: First set a plan. If you have your own consistent position, you must have a consistent path. You won't be translating "Infantry Drill Manual" today and "The Renaissance" tomorrow. The plan can be centered on an era or centered on an idea. First translate X, then translate Y, with a definite step-by-step approach. It is best to take the modern Chinese readership as a prerequisite. Your writing style is too profound, making it difficult for people to understand; or you translate works that are irrelevant to us, such as "The History of Fashion Changes in Paris over the Past Forty Years" or "Research on London Fog," which are beautiful, but what is it to China! "What is it to the people!"

Generally, if the aim is established and the ability is also very high, then at this time there is the question of "how to translate." The above three items all explain "how to be qualified to translate books." The following points discuss how to translate to achieve twice the result with half the effort: 1. Do not translate English-Chinese dictionaries, or French-Chinese dictionaries, etc.—When using dictionaries when translating, it is best to use dictionaries that provide the original text's original explanation. Most of the current foreign language-Chinese dictionaries are suitable for beginners of foreign languages, but not suitable for translation. Sometimes when your train of thought is stuck, seeking inspiration in such dictionaries is like a restless hope for comfort from the opposite sex, who only makes you more restless and inflamed. What poet who writes well would embrace the "Peiwen Yunfu" or "Shiyun Hebi"?

What translator constantly takes out words from the dictionary to patch together and arrange? Moreover, the existing foreign language-Chinese dictionaries are mostly confused to the point of being hopeless.

Last Words 233

— Lin Huiyin

"Oh, sympathy!" A sharp tremor pierced her heart.

Yina decided to write a letter to those who were good at sympathy. She took out a pen and a handkerchief from her handbag, and then exchanged this handbag for the equipment needed to write the letter.

Near the Cathay Theatre, she walked into a delicate coffee shop. She ordered a cup of coffee and began to write. To those who are good at sympathy:

"Yes, I am a weak person, but I don't want your sympathy, much less your pity. Also, if you want to be sentimental, please let go of this weak person and find another object, how about it?

She wanted to write a few more sentences, but she couldn't think of what to write. She opened the envelope, addressed to Xi Zhuoyun. She also wanted to write a letter to him, telling him that this was her last submission and asking him to publish it as soon as possible. But she didn't write. She didn't write anything else, only her name under the title.

The coffee was cold. She drank it all in one gulp and went to the nearest post office to send the letter by registered mail.

Leaving the post office, she walked west. She was paying attention to where the trams were running faster. She walked all the way past the Huida Hotel and stopped in front of the French barracks.

Seeing a beautiful No. 2 tram speeding over, she ran over and threw herself forward onto the tracks.

Undoubtedly, by the time the letter had been mailed, Yina had already entered another world, making that letter a will. (The End)
