Shen Bao Local Supplement

Conversations

This Ambition Is Frightening 234

— Meng Ruo

China, surrounded by powerful nations, is like a piece of fat meat, which everyone is drooling over. Today, Country A fantasizes about digging a hole, tomorrow Country B attempts to take a few bites. Up to now, the reason why it has been fortunate enough to barely survive is not because it has any resistance of its own, but because the ambitious people have not yet finished dividing it up. However, even if it is being swallowed piece by piece like this, I am afraid that one day it will be eaten up completely!

We see that Outer Mongolia has long declared independence, the Northeast is no longer ours, Inner Mongolia is just now making a fuss about demanding autonomy, and alarming news continues to come from Tibet and Xinjiang. The outbreak of all these unfortunate events is invariably instigated by ambitious people behind the scenes, who are playing tricks and conspiracies. In order to prevent fires from starting, they seem to have secretly agreed on a plan and are colluding with each other, tacitly acknowledging a certain place as a certain country's sphere of influence, and a certain place as a certain person's area of activity. In this way, each country can freely and unrestrictedly charge around in its so-called sphere of influence or area of activity, doing whatever it wants. As long as it does not hinder the interests of other countries, no one will come out to interfere. Not only that, but sometimes after they have trampled on something to their satisfaction, they will turn around and do a favor, currying favor and inciting others to commit aggression, which is hateful and detestable! The following news is a major exposure of Japanese conspiracies.

According to reports from Moscow, the former Turkish Prince Abdülkerim has departed from Shanghai for Xinjiang. Kerim went to Shanghai from Tokyo a few months ago and hid in a certain concession. He is a puppet of Japan and a candidate for the throne of an independent kingdom in Xinjiang. Currently, some Japanese military circles are cooperating with Turkish exiles to actively win over military and propaganda cadres in order to promote the realization of an independent kingdom in Xinjiang. According to the report, Kerim's departure from Shanghai is to personally preside over this work, as the work has already made considerable progress (TASS dispatch on the 23rd).

After reading this alarming news, I feel that the ambition of the Japanese is very frightening. Since they coerced our country into signing the Twenty-One Demands, they have used every means to deal with our country. The September 18th Incident saw them extend a huge palm and forcibly seize the land of our four provinces, establishing their so-called Manchuria. We thought that since they had obtained this "lifeline," and their long-cherished desire had been fulfilled, they might somewhat curb their ambitious aggression. Who knew that the enemy's greed was insatiable, and they would take an inch and demand a mile? There was first the attempt to organize a North China nation, and now there is the conspiracy to incite the former Prince to go to Xinjiang to establish an independent nation. Their premeditation is also vicious! Although it has not yet been verified whether this cable is reliable, our country should not remain indifferent at a time when the Xinjiang dispute has not been resolved. I hope that our government and people will pay close attention to this and prevent ambitious people from achieving their improper goals, which would cause great losses and disasters!

Meddling 235

— Yi Ping

Friends intentionally or unintentionally ask me why I haven't been writing recently. Because I am a person who makes a living by writing, suddenly stopping writing seems surprising to them. Of course, they are too embarrassed to ask me if I haven't been eating recently, but the tone of the question seems to contain an attempt to uncover my secrets. Since I accidentally wrote a few love stories last year, friends have had a lot of talking points. Young people are naturally energetic when talking about love, especially when they enjoy uncovering other people's secrets. In fact, I am a law-abiding young man, and I can no longer be interested in love. Although I was somewhat moved by Miss Fei after meeting her, she has already gone to the South. We met unintentionally and parted just as unintentionally. However, my accusation seems to have been established because of this: a young man who writes love stories must be in love. So, I was suspected by my friends, so I thought I would never write such articles again. Having made such a decision, I wandered around every day, taking the opportunity to rest from my hard work over the past year, and then work hard to write. However, not writing can also make friends distrust me. Recently, friends who asked me the reason for not writing also added a sentence: What are you busy with? Obviously, he thought that the reason for not writing was being restrained by something, and that something was the secret they wanted to uncover. To borrow an old saying, "No coincidence, no story." A friend visited me three times and didn't find me at home. Yesterday, I met him in the cinema. I happened to be with a lady whom I had only met once and had forgotten her name (actually, everyone may have encountered this kind of embarrassing situation). He questioned me as if he had caught me red-handed. I felt very bored in that situation. At the same time, I felt very sorry for the lady whose name I didn't know, who was being ridiculed when she was confused.

The nature of the Chinese is to like to meddle in other people's business. They often eat their own fill and worry about other people's accounts. The young lady of the East family is unruly, the daughter-in-law of the West family is having an affair, as if he were involved, and he can give a full and satisfying account from beginning to end. Especially for this kind of scandalous affair that is considered a secret, he can add fuel to the fire and make it sensational. The person who is speaking is indeed satisfied with his desire to destroy, but those who meddle should also be prepared for when their own business is meddled in, and they probably wouldn't be happy if others did that to them, right? Furthermore, going to a movie with a girlfriend is, in my opinion, nothing surprising, even though the cinema in Shanghai is not a good place.

I have been meddled with from my hometown to Shanghai, making it impossible for me to ever return to my old nest, which is within sight. My fate seems to be controlled by the hands of those who meddle, so I hate meddling as much as others like to meddle.

However, to tell the truth, that friend didn't necessarily intend to meddle in my business. He eats the same white rice as me, and moreover, his own business is also being meddled in by others. Joking around is certainly acceptable between friends, but I don't need you to do my advertising for me! Perhaps I am going to offend my friends, but that is not my hope; I am going to write, and hereby announce that I am not restrained by anything like a secret.

Page 20

A Certain Death 236

— Lie Huo

Death is common, but the death of Hu, even though it has been three long years, still weighs heavily on my mind. I cannot forget him, his shadow is always flickering before my eyes, because his death was too tragic! Because his death was too unjust! But he did not die in a domestic quarrel, nor did he die under the gun of a suspected criminal for an unprovable charge, and he did not die from economic oppression, or even suicide from unrequited love.

He died of illness, truly and certainly.

On a larger scale, his death was due to feudal forces, and his parents directly wielded the executioner's blade; however, his parents were indeed the most loving towards him - they saw him as a precious pearl in the palm of their hand. So, although they ended their son's life, they were almost driven mad by Hu's death.

This is a contradictory thing, and even more contradictory death!

If there really is such a thing as "genius" in human talent, then I would call Hu a child genius. He was the most outstanding of my childhood friends. Eleven years ago, we studied together in the same private school, reading things like the Selections of Refined Literature and Comprehensive Mirror to Aid in Governance, all of which he could recite fluently. At that time, he was only twelve years old. Later, we went to high school together, and his homework was always more proficient than others. Although not every exam result showed it, his name always fell far behind ours.

In terms of physique, his inherent body - the frame his parents gave him - although not very strong, was not weaker than that of ordinary children. Compared to me, he was probably slightly better.

When we graduated from high school, he was only fifteen years old. According to physiology, it was the peak of puberty. He did grow quickly. One time he told me, "I'm getting married soon, probably before going to the provincial capital to study!" Naturally, at that time, I was also like a "mouse greeting the light," unable to see that early marriage was harmful; and in our hometown, early marriage had become common practice. As long as a family had food to eat, children as young as thirteen or fourteen, still "wet behind the ears," would get married, and the women they married were in their twenties. So, when I heard what he said, I not only did not disapprove, but also admired it a little.

Little did I know that this was the root of Hu's early death.

When we went to City C to study, we were in different schools. Because we were far apart, and because we were both still studying hard, we did not see each other often. Only occasionally did I hear some news about him from other moving friends - that he was often sick, and it was said that he had contracted tuberculosis. So, I worried about him, and I considered his life journey. When I returned home for vacation, I gave him some advice - not to be harmed by his wife, and that "avoiding sex" was the only panacea for curing his illness, but I don't know if he ever took my advice.

In 1928, we came to Shanghai together, with the aim of taking the entrance exam for the X Public School, which has now been discontinued. His wife also came with him. He himself was willing, and his parents did not object. The friends' persuasion, of course, was like the "wind in the ear," having no effect at all. Unfortunately, he did not pass the exam, suffering a setback, and he continued to spend every day with his wife. At this time, in addition to being infected by the feudal poison of his hometown, he was also tempted by the "romance" of the city, and his body could not support it. So, he returned to his hometown.

In the spring of 1929, he wrote to me with two pieces of news - one was that his original wife had passed away due to childbirth complications, and the other was that he had married a "fairly suitable" second wife. That was terrible, and I could only feel more worried for him, but I had nothing to say, because saying it would be ineffective. His parents were both so ignorant.

In the summer of 1931, I returned to my hometown and specially went to visit him. He was already a corpse before the god of death. His stomach was swollen like a tadpole's belly, his face was pale, and when I talked to him, he only burst into sobs. His parents sat beside him, recounting the past few years in detail, with tears and snot streaming down their faces.

A week later, the news of his death reached my ears.

Hu died like this. It was a tragic death! A truly unjust death! But in our hometown, and even in the vast and closed interior, many young people suffer from the feudal poison, recklessly marry early, and die such tragic and unjust deaths!

Healthy Queen 237

— Che Tian

(Beiping News: The queen election scene involved over two hundred female students competing, parading in formation. Initially, over thirty were selected, followed by a second round of voting resulting in five finalists. Finally, after careful deliberation and evaluation by the judges, the "Healthy Queen" crown was awarded to "Wu XX", a second-year medical student. The entire venue erupted in cheers, and the Department of Physical Education presented her with flowers as a reward...)

Originally, it seems this year has taken a bit of a "turn backward," like a retro trend causing a "queen craze."

In the past, there were movie queens, school queens, courtesan queens, and... various other queens of unclear nature. In this environment where "where there's testing, there's cheating," queen elections inevitably involve corruption. Perhaps there are exceptions, but please forgive my exaggeration.

In short, whether or not there's corruption is a separate issue. Those who can ascend to the queen's throne must possess unique qualities. At the very least, they must meet one of the following two criteria:

(1) A lithe figure and a beautiful face.

(2) Eloquent speech and frivolous demeanor.

Indeed, we are accustomed to seeing such figures, like a monkey show. To summarize, those elected are merely embracing "show-offism." As for the electors, even if they don't dare to have "ulterior motives," they at least have "private agendas"! Ask yourself, would an old woman have the qualifications to be elected queen?

Therefore, when newspapers reveal their names and publish commercialized, leisurely writing about them, I simply consider them as yet another expensive, distinctive, and valuable vase in society!

Now, Miss "Wu XX" has been elected queen. Because she is the "Healthy Queen," I think she is ultimately more insightful and meaningful than other queens. At the very least, Miss Wu carries the mission of being a "healthy role model," attracting Chinese women to pursue health, which is much better than "university queens" who only engage in romance with male students and create chaos, or romantic "movie queens" who merely cut ribbons at opening ceremonies.

Finally, I hope this is an honest election, without any attached purposes! Then, the "Healthy Queen" would truly be worthy of praise!

I don't know what others think, but I always find the word "queen" too vulgar and a bit too retro. Perhaps it's because "things reach an extreme only to revert," and everyone wants to taste the flavors of the past. Unable to taste the actual flavors, they settle for hanging an ancient sign, considering it a small indulgence. It's like being born in this era and hearing elders say how good ancient times were. Although we haven't witnessed it, we secretly hope to live in such a peaceful century, enjoying a couple of years of peace. However, we can only indulge in dreams, like hanging an "ancient queen sign." Perhaps it's possible, but who can predict such things? After rambling on, I wonder if those who aspire to be "queen" share the same sentiment. This is a very interesting question worth studying!

The Wandering Child Fu (16) 238

— Chen Jingsheng

Poor thing! The motherless orphan's mother died, and now the enemy is coming to bomb our poor children?

Standing Outside the Ranks of Children 239

— Hutu

The clear sky is swept by gusts of slightly chilly wind, and golden sunlight shines over the land. The branches of the roadside trees have already sprouted pale green buds, and the willow branches sway with graceful姿态 in the gentle breeze. From the depths of my mind, I deeply realize: spring has arrived in the world! Thus, with a heart full of fervent emotions, sincerely and earnestly, I went to the virgin-like, serene Zhaofeng Park to seek the traces of the god of spring.

Indeed, spring is lovely. But especially in this neatly trimmed, clean park, the green grass, lush shade of trees, clear small pond, and layered rockeries... everything feels worthy of admiration.

Walking to the fishpond, I saw a group of children sitting on a green lawn, full of life, so innocent and so lovely. Seeing the small flags in their hands, I realized that they were led out to play by their teachers from school. In the embrace of nature, they ate food and chatted and played, like a herd of released horses or a flock of docile lambs, playing together under the leadership of their teachers. How happy!

I recalled my childhood days, when I was just as happy and carefree as they were! However, years have passed, and the sweet dreams of the golden age will never return. At this moment, a feeling of longing is truly indescribable! I wished I could join their ranks, laugh and play with them. Finally, I raised my voice and shouted: "Children! Can I join your ranks? Children! Please let me join your ranks!" But none of them paid attention to me. Several times I shouted like this, but none of them paid attention to me. After eating well, they sat for a while, got up from the grass, and went outside in a long line.

Ah! A discarded heart, having lost its innocence, stood outside the ranks of children, pacing back and forth, its heart filled with sadness and pain. Tears streamed down from my eyes, wetting my clothes, but I didn't notice. I only deeply felt: "Now I can only stand outside the ranks of children!"

The Problem of Marriage Between Close Relatives 240

— Lüsha

Marriage between close relatives has adverse effects on offspring. This is what most scholars have been advocating recently, such as deafness, muteness, deformities, idiocy, pigmentary retinitis, and weak constitutions, which are often seen in the descendants of those who marry within close bloodlines. Scholars have already made many reports. But I think they have absolutely no scientific basis. Why? If marriage between close relatives has such a detrimental effect on offspring, then the people of ancient times, who always had the habit of marrying within close relationships, wouldn't their descendants be very weak? But the facts tell us that this is not the case. In ancient times, such as in Egypt and Persia, the nobility married within close relatives. For example, Cleopatra, the Queen of Egypt, was one of the most beautiful women in the world, born from a marriage between siblings. Not only did she have a strong physique, but she also had a clear and intelligent mind, capable of freely using the dialects of eighteen countries and being proficient in Greek literature and philosophy. Even the scholars of that time felt that she was behind them. Furthermore, marriage between close relatives is still prevalent in modern Japan, especially among the imperial family. Are they all mentally disabled, idiotic, or deformed?

But then again, why has marriage between close relatives always been criticized by scholars? That's all based on hearsay. Originally, the characteristics of our bodies and minds, as well as the predisposing factors and constitutions to diseases, can be inherited by offspring. In those who marry from the same bloodline, the peculiarities existing between their bloodlines, whether good or bad, will have a more intense influence on their descendants. Therefore, if the bloodline is strong, marriage between close relatives is beneficial to offspring. Conversely, if the bloodline still has hereditary diseases or is weak, then marriage between bloodlines is harmful to offspring. However, to go a step further: it is rare to find a bloodline with both healthy body and mind. Therefore, when bloodlines marry each other for generations, their descendants will inevitably suffer from the influence of heredity. Except for bloodlines that are physically strong and have absolutely no hereditary constitutions, it is still better to avoid marriage between close relatives. In summary, deafness, muteness, idiocy, and weakness are definitely not the causes of marriage between close relatives. From the principle of heredity, it is the influence of special hereditary defects in the bloodline being doubled and passed on to descendants. We absolutely cannot believe those theories that marriage between close relatives directly deteriorates the blood and causes various diseases.

In conclusion, marriage between close relatives is not harmful if there are no aforementioned illnesses. However, marrying within bloodlines for generations is detrimental to offspring.

Page 21

Minor Illness 241

— Wenli

Busy people like to have minor illnesses to rest their tired bodies. I, an unbusy person, am now having a minor illness, which is as annoying as a child born into a large family. I've been sick for days, unable to read or write at home, and staring at the white wall all day long. In my discomfort, I've had many beautiful daydreams. The central idea of the stories is: if one day I could have food to eat without having to write, any occupation would be fine. It's as if I'm inside a movie screen, sometimes a schoolteacher lecturing students on an introduction to literature, sometimes a clerk in a newspaper office copying documents, sometimes an accountant in a store recording accounts and writing letters... It's as if I've become someone who isn't unemployed, how proud! But at the same time, I think about what would happen if a minor illness turned into a major one. Thinking of this, the scene of visiting a friend at the Red Cross hospital the other day immediately began to play in my mind like a movie screen, scene by scene. The third-class room with more than a dozen beds filled with moaning patients, the camera: from far to near, arriving at my friend's bed. Close-up: my friend's withered, pale, bloodless face, his eyes barely open, his dry lips moving as he speaks, but with little strength. Subtitle: "I've been sick for a month or two, spent a lot of money, but the illness hasn't improved at all! Now I have no money, I owe the hospital, what am I going to do?" I only spoke a few words to him when I saw the nurse coming. She forbade the patient to talk. Close-up: the nurse's angry face, glaring at the patient and scolding. Subtitle: "You're not allowed to talk, the doctor ordered it, you never listen! I won't let anyone visit you anymore!" As she said this, she glanced at me, explaining that he wasn't allowed to talk. Subtitle: "Those of you who come to visit should stop him from talking." As she said this, she twisted her waist and walked away. I thought to myself: why be so arrogant to a patient? Wouldn't it be better to be kinder? Recalling, near shot: in a first-class ward, I was also visiting a sick friend. A nurse came in, smiling kindly and speaking to the patient. Subtitle: "Mr. X, you have to be obedient, the doctor told you not to talk too much. Why did you talk so much as soon as your friend came? Don't do it again, ah, ah, listen to me." The patient felt happy and promised her that he wouldn't talk too much anymore, and I admired her dedication to her duties. Back to the third-class room, near shot: I saw my sick friend, having been scolded by the nurse, looked at me. Saying "Patients who owe money are often subjected to such treatment, alas!" One (character) Close-up: On my friend's face, tears welled up and fell from his eyes... Thinking of that ward, I shuddered. My heart was praying: please don't let me get a serious illness.

A serious illness for a poor person is like being half dead, I'm afraid.

Eugenics 242

— Qisu

"Dragons beget dragons, phoenixes beget phoenixes, thieves raise sons who dig holes in walls." This is a common saying: it means that the emperor's son must be the crown prince, the big boss's son can't but be a "young master," and those born to poor people must be "lowly." However, the facts tell us that Jie and Zhou both served as the emperor's sons: The father of Emperor Xuantong was also a direct descendant of the Qing Dynasty: Moreover, there are also many who have once caused a stir who have been to Zhengjia Muqiao to ask a real young master. On the contrary, the backgrounds of today's so-called "tycoons" who ride in cars and eat gourmet food cannot necessarily be celebrated in writing. Therefore, this theory of the common saying is rarely heard from the mouths of ordinary clever people.

Instead, one often hears talk of how the breed of dogs cannot be mixed, as it will only turn bad: also, the breed of pigeons is also very particular. And the sons of the strong will ultimately be healthier. This originally relates to the innate and is, of course, an ironclad theory. However, some people once argued that the reason why a certain lady was able to make a great splash in the national games with her sprint was because her ancestors, for business reasons, had to run from Guannei to Guanwai several times a year on foot, which trained her strong elements and passed them on to her, which is somewhat puzzling. Because we believe that "environment" is the biggest reason for a person's failure and success. For example, if a certain lady had been locked up in a tower by her parents since she was a child, becoming a complete virgin, would she have the possibility of becoming famous for sprinting? Or, if a certain lady had been born into a poor family and spent her days washing rice, washing vegetables, and carrying children, without the good fortune to study at school and never understanding how to start a sprint, would she have stood out at the games? The various relationships in society, the so-called environment, determine everything, and no one can ride a auspicious cloud, leaving the ground.

Some people also believe that, in addition to a strong physique, outstanding spirit, noble personality, and solemn morality also have hereditary properties. Therefore, they proposed finding ways to allow noble people to leave more descendants, and to pay attention to the child-rearing of all base, vulgar, and mediocre people, so that future society would be full of good seeds and no evil would occur.

But this is also an equally untenable theory. The relations of production in society, that is, economic conditions, determine everything. Reason and will cannot control people in the slightest. A famous scientist, for the sake of his stomach, would manufacture lethal weapons, and a virtuous preacher, in order to be comfortable, could deceive goats for cunning foxes. The iron circle of economics dominates those within the circle. There will be no exceptions, and there will be no coincidences.

Anyone who is truly worried about the "world" and wants to remedy it, then they only have to pick up a broom and sweep the environment. There is no need to ride an auspicious cloud, fly in the air, or learn the wonderful skills of the Monkey King.

Woman 243

— Gaoren

"When you ask to kiss a woman, she has been waiting for you for a long time." Probably like that, I remember someone said.

To seize a woman's heart seems so easy; However, no—

"When you bring flowers to the home of the one you love, she is already nestled in the arms of another man."

Mentioning women, I want to destroy the world: although I am still a man who needs women.

Many women have left me. I didn't ask to kiss them, I don't know if they had waited for me for a long time; I didn't bring flowers to their homes: but they were already in the arms of other men.

I know too few women: at the same time, I know too many women.

Hearing young people talking about women—I am also young—I want to speak, but I am silent. I played so many love tricks, I woke up like from a dream: I should love my wife—that only woman snuggling in my arms—but— Woman—a woman I thought was a little girl, when I loved her like I love my daughter, she learned to be like a mother, she wrote me a letter with only a few words—"She loves me—"

"What to do? She is a woman!" I thought about it and finally accepted it.

The love of a little girl is pure. Her loving me is not necessarily the same as other women loving me, I need a daughter who loves her father, and I finally accepted it.

The father-daughter love began.

— Summer of 1933.

On the large lawn of the French Park, two were telling the stories of princes and princesses. On Avenue Joffre, two figures strolled aimlessly. Inside the movie theater, four eyes watched the changes on the screen.

She loves me, I love her: a daughter and a father.

The news of the daughter's marriage spread, she cried in my arms like a mother, her eyes were swollen from crying, and she shouted about suicide.

"Daughter, you should have a young man to accompany you, Daddy has a mother." I patted her shoulder and widened my eyes to tell her what that meant.

She gave me a grateful hot kiss—I didn't wait for her for a long time, and she floated away like a planet.

Losing a daughter, the father did not have the sadness of losing a mother—a daughter should have a young man to accompany her.

END Before the conversation began, an unexpected episode.

— Spring of 1934.

The daughter and her husband returned, a young couple. She told me that she was very painful, her husband did not understand women, and she still loved me.

The father smiled helplessly, he could no longer caress his daughter as before, and he could no longer snatch his daughter into his arms.

The daughter was already a mother-like woman.

Phone calls connected to letters, letters connected to phone calls, disturbing an old man's heart, and the daughter's husband also began to suspect her father...

...Mentioning women, I want to destroy this world; although I am still a man who needs women.

Woman啊!

Written on February 20, 1934 in a small building.

Youth Needs "Understanding" 244

— Jianshe

Spiritual decadence has become a common ailment among young people, popularly dominating everyone's thoughts and behaviors. Therefore, I think this is a problem worth discussing, because it concerns us so closely.

Why is our spirit decadent? Some people think it's due to physical weakness and congenital heredity, so they elaborate: the vigor or decadence of the spirit is due to the strength or weakness of the body, such as the physical strength of the body. A strong body has great physical strength, and a weak body has little physical strength. The spirit is also the same, a strong body has a vigorous spirit, and a weak body has a decadent spirit. Then, they further explain the causes of physical weakness: first, due to illness, and second, due to congenital heredity. So the conclusion is that if you want the spirit to not be decadent, you must first strengthen the body.

On this, I disagree. Of course, the strength or weakness of the body can have a considerable influence on the spirit. But if we carefully observe the phenomenon of youth decadence, I feel that "understanding" is the most important factor in it. The blindness, mistakes, and many unfortunate things arising from blindness and mistakes are probably due to the lack of thorough understanding. The primitive people's worship of nature, the medieval people's bowing down to idols, ... are all due to not understanding the truth of these things. We know that so-called understanding is to analyze and observe something with extensive knowledge, far-sighted vision, and meticulous thinking. The clearer the analysis, the deeper the observation, the more thorough the work of understanding. With understanding as a tool, we can uncover the shrouds of all things and all phenomena: we can get close to the truth of the event.

We analyze the phenomenon of youth spiritual decadence and feel that it is not due to physical weakness, nor is it congenital heredity: but because the three problems of "love," "occupation," and "thought" cannot be solved. Among these three, the thought problem is the most important. As long as one of these three problems is violated, a young person can be decadent, and a living man can become a desolate and depressed person out of thin air. To avoid this decadent fate, one must find the fundamental driving force of this current society. The current society is undoubtedly a society full of contradictions and darkness. In this society, money has become the supreme ruler of mankind. This ruler derives many systems, inspections, military preparations, laws, etc., which suppress us, so that our young men and women, even with enthusiasm, cannot find a lover; even with a lover, they cannot be together; they make us sell ourselves cheaply, but we are often subjected to the doom of unemployment. As a result, we feel that this world is full of darkness, and we seem to have lost our guides, constantly hesitating and shaking.

In such a world, if we do not have a far-sighted vision and understand that the current situation, although full of contradictions and darkness, is only the inevitable phenomenon of the development of an old social system to its highest degree, to the eve of its collapse. Then we can easily be threatened and controlled by this dark side, and as a result, we will become gray, decadent, and defeated. So in the meantime, it's just a question of understanding or not understanding, and nothing else.

If we can truly understand the current society, then we can know that the attacks on love and the uncompensated exploitation of intelligence and physical strength are due to the unreasonable and bad social system. If we further know from historical investigation that this society is not fixed but evolving, and that a social system must collapse when it develops to a certain stage, then we can not only know the reasons for our pain, disappointment, and defeat, but also decide our own thoughts, so that in the face of this era's turbulent current, we know which side we should lean towards, and not make ourselves a straggler without a way out or a future.

How can we achieve these? It's all because of our understanding of reality.

Therefore, I feel that the strength or weakness of the body is not what determines our fate of decadence or non-decadence: on the contrary, understanding or not understanding is the fundamental reason for determining it. Therefore, I feel that if we want to wipe out the problem of our youth decadence, we only need to work harder on understanding.

Novel

Siamese Ramblings 245

— Yi Min

(Introduction)

My trip to Siam was in the winter of 1929. Shanghai had already experienced snowfall. Shivering from the cold, I boarded the Taikoo Company's Nan Hua ship. As the ship crossed the Taiwan Strait, the weather gradually warmed up. By the third day when we landed in Shantou, the passengers had already shed their winter clothes and donned light autumn attire. I had never been to the South before and was amazed at how the climate could be so different in just three days. At the time, I felt like a country bumpkin who had never seen the world, full of surprise and admiration upon entering a bustling metropolis!

Coincidentally, there was a Siam-bound ship departing that day. I only stayed in Shantou for a few hours before embarking on another long sea voyage. The journey from Shantou to Siam usually takes a week, but it could take ten days if the seas were rough. I was on one of the faster ships on the Shantou-Siam route, so I only spent six days on board. For the first day or two, I didn't feel much, but after seeing the Annam Mountains, the weather became hotter every moment. First, I couldn't wear my coat, then I took off my vest and trousers. By the last day or two, even I, who was usually sensitive to the cold, had to follow others in dousing myself with cold water. This was a very ordinary thing for those who grew up in the tropics, but for me, it was a miracle!

Now, it's another severe winter with continuous wind and snow. I'm wrapped in bulky winter clothes, with the doors and windows tightly closed, yet I still don't feel warm. So, Siam, where it's summer all year round, evokes my memories again, and that's the motivation for writing this piece. The following observations are based on our experiences during our two-year stay in Siam. I think it might provide a useful reference for readers who are concerned about the current situation of the Chinese community in Siam, and also leave a lasting impression for myself.

Movie Special

Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer Used a Replacement Plan So Garbo Had No Choice But to Return to America (Part 1) 246

— Guang Dao

It's probably been over a year since Garbo returned to Hollywood. The reason for her return to America is still a matter of debate. Recently, an article was published in the American "Screen Play" magazine, describing the reason why this Swedish star suddenly returned to the United States. I found it interesting and because it revealed something that hadn't been discussed before, I excerpted some of it for the readers.

Among Greta Garbo's closest friends, they all knew that when she left Hollywood last time and returned to her native Sweden, she had intended to retire. She had even bought a large villa, intending to spend her remaining years in her hometown. Although America was the place where she became famous and rich, in her passionate soul, she loathed America the most and had no intention of returning to Hollywood. In the Swedish countryside villa, she could find quiet comfort and escape the scrutiny of all the strange eyes. At that time, her intention to retire was very firm. The Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer company, of course, did not fully understand this. They knew that she had no intention of returning to the screen, so they sent out scouts to find her replacement. As a result, they found a Russian dancer. She had no experience on screen, but she had a foreign exotic and seductive personality, with the potential to develop and replace Garbo. Therefore, Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer, of course, did not hesitate to sign a contract with her and secretly brought her back to the United States.

Who is this Russian singer? Her name is Kathryn Seava.

She has yellow hair and blue eyes. She has all the exotic charm and radiance that Russian women possess. Her face resembles Garbo's. After Garbo returned to Sweden, rumors of Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer seeking a replacement for Garbo were rampant. Ambitious women, hearing that the title of movie queen was still vacant, developed a desire to compete, as long as there was some resemblance in their features. But among these contenders, no one resembled Garbo as closely as Kathryn Seava. Her square face, with slightly exposed cheekbones, and her eyes, nose, and mouth, all resembled the Swedish Garbo. Someone saw her, and the way she walked was so similar that some people mistook her for Garbo herself.

Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer had big plans for this Ms. Seava. They decided that if Greta Garbo did not return to America, they would promote Ms. Seava and make her a star overnight, just like Samuel Goldwyn promoted another new Russian star, Anna Sten, in a surprising and amazing way. They did not want to waste her on small roles and let her slowly rise to stardom step by step. They deliberately concealed her, keeping it a secret from the outside world, and then when the time was right, they would promote her and give her a big boost. (To be continued)

Talking About Films

Review of "Fashions of 1934" 247

— Ling He

Fashions of 1934—Nanjing—

Following "42nd Street," "Gold Diggers of 1933," and "Roman Scandals," a series of musicals have emerged one after another in a dazzling array. Here comes another one, "Fashions of 1934," which is obviously another typical American musical.

We can almost certainly say that the expressive methods of American film art have indeed reached their peak. It can be said that in some American films, we can see the highest form of capitalist cinema. In musicals, "Gold Diggers of 1933" is like that, "Roman Scandals" is like that, and now "Fashions of 1934" is also like that. It is the most highly formalistic work.

After watching this film, we might as well close our eyes and think quietly: how desperately are American filmmakers spending money? When we see the feather fan dance, the emptiness of beauty inlaid with gold is certainly not enough to make us envious or intoxicated, but the waste of capitalism is something we can't imagine. Of course, we don't need that kind of decadent luxury in our films, but we must recognize that it is a characteristic of capitalist cinema.

Similarly, a bright and joyful tone is a new feature of American films, and these are also fully and unreservedly displayed in "Fashions of 1934." From this point of view, we can see the director's clever and lively technique even more. The whole thing is a bright rhythm. Every joke is natural and develops without pretense. There is hardly a scene that can give you a chance to feel bored. Naturally, this will feel very comfortable for tired city dwellers. Precisely because of this, the director can give you what you want, and so the director has indeed succeeded in that aspect.

Ladies and gentlemen, please be happy to your heart's content. At least while watching this film, you can forget the painful reality. When you leave the theater and return to the unpleasant reality, you may as well cry to your heart's content. However, drinking to drown your sorrows is a good way to relieve boredom. Now you might as well use the appreciation of musical films to replace the stimulation of alcohol. This is the most reasonable reason why bright musicals are so popular. Of course, this is the social basis for making films similar to "Fashions of 1934."

Generally speaking, ordinary musicals do not pay attention to the substance of the content. "Fashions of 1934" is no exception. However, the playwright reflects a little bit of reality. When Nash (played by William Powell) fails in his speculation, we cannot help but think of the fact that the foundation of the old society is shaking has become a widespread phenomenon. However, in this situation, the people who suffer the most are ultimately the people in the lower class. The so-called exploiters of the upper class are not willing to give up and will eventually come up with another new speculative method to maintain their own position. Even cheating and trickery are used without hesitation. Originally, in this false and treacherous society, everything is self-deception. Especially in this panic, as long as you have the ability to deceive, you might as well show it off as much as possible. Deception, theft, fraud, do anything. However, as the saying goes, "there is always someone stronger than you." While you are deceiving others, you will also be deceived by others. Regarding this point, the playwright writes that Nash's mistress took two thousand dollars from him, but it was stolen by Snap (played by Frank McHugh). Snap was complacent, but unexpectedly it fell into Nash's hands without him knowing. In addition, he also vividly describes the psychology of businessmen. Doria and others denounced Nash for counterfeiting fashion, but Nash asked them to fund his trip to Paris to plagiarize new fashion styles. At the time, Doria and others strongly refused, but soon each of them signed a contract with him privately. This proves how selfish and contradictory realistic businessmen are. Secondly, in the White Russian Duchess or the rich man Bullock, the ugliness of noble people is also fully exposed.

As mentioned above, the playwright uses a lively and satirical style, which is extremely vivid, humorous, and scolding, which can be said to be excellent. And the director understands the script in this way, and with the help of extremely bright directing techniques, "Fashions of 1934" has achieved great success. As for the liveliness of the camera, it is even more superfluous.

Of course, it is very appropriate to have William Powell play the con man Nash. At the same time, Frank McHugh, who collaborated with him in "One Way Passage," still uses that kind of sneer here, but it is not as well-coordinated with the plot as in "One Way Passage." As for the female roles, there is not much to praise. The one who plays the White Russian Duchess is still acceptable, but has no special strengths. The others are just passable.

Review of "The Bell Rings" 248

— Ya Fu

—Jin Cheng Film—

Revolution, revolution, these two words have indeed been shouted very loudly and sound very nice in recent years. Isn't that so? Take the revolution of the sixteenth year of the Republic as an example. Many people died heroically in the torrent of blood, while at the same time, many people prospered and were promoted by sucking the bright red blood.

What is even more terrible is those people who are used to putting up a sheep's head and selling dog meat, carrying the banner of revolution and implementing the reality of false revolution. They even sing loudly about propriety, justice, integrity, and shame, but in reality, they use masks to cover up their ugliness. Alas! Revolution, revolution, "how many sins are committed in your name."

"The Bell Rings," judging from the words, I think there must be many great stories. However, reality is often not as beautiful as imagination. After watching this film, we can't help but feel greatly disappointed.

Naturally, what we must examine is the development of the story. We need revolution, this is an ironclad fact. Especially the result of the warlord melee pointed out in the film, the vast majority of people are suffering. Therefore, at this time, only the power of revolution can destroy everything old and allow the new society to grow in a new economic structure. But how does the playwright explain this era? He said: "Brave young men should serve the country with their lives" and not talk about love. Just ring the alarm bells a few times, let the young masters be plainclothes police, and cooperate from the inside and outside to respond to the National Revolution. It is possible to "successfully revolutionize" at once. (This refers to the revolution of the sixteenth year of the Republic) And what happens after success? The playwright tells us that machines are produced and a large number of workers have work to do. How distorted is this reality! However, the author explained that it was a group of young students' tricks. I think this is a faithful confession.

Let's leave this point aside and see how the playwright promotes his feudal ideas. He advocates emulating Liu, Guan, and Zhang's brotherhood. There are actually three young people bowing to three Bodhisattvas, and the result is "brothers of different surnames are closer than blood."

Speaking of Wen Yimin's directing skills, then we can say that the first half is not without merit, but it doesn't work later. Let's see, he has spent a lot of effort on the composition of each picture, and even the montage within the picture. Compared with previous works, there is also progress. However, the editing of the picture is not very reasonable. For example, when the story begins, the relationship between Zhenzhen's father and son and Qianghua Middle School is not well introduced. It is not until the end of the film that people understand their relationship. However, there are many places that are very concise before and after this. Later, there are more and more weaknesses, such as Zhenzhen buying medicine at the pharmacy and suddenly writing about a rich lady buying perfume. There is no close connection beforehand, and it is not until Zhenzhen picks up a dollar that people understand his intention. Also, after Zhenzhen met Li Cangsheng, he used a large subtitle to replace a process. In fact, the explanation of this process is not difficult. Why use subtitles to replace the picture?

As mentioned earlier, we can see the director's intelligence in some places (of course, there are many small flaws), but when we recognize that a director should be responsible for the entire film, we hope that he will not be too casual in the selection of scripts, and must be careful and prudent.

Now, regarding acting skills, we believe that Fan Xuepeng has many good performances when playing a little girl. Her playful and lively demeanor is indeed commendable. After marrying Li Cangsheng, she is completely acting in a twisted and unnatural way, without any sense of reality. Needless to say, the director should also be responsible for this. Yao Yi is very young and acts very calmly. As for the same white hat after four years, the director was again careless. Li Yun, who plays Li Cangsheng, is also passable.

Finally, what must be said is that photography and scenery are all symbols of Qianghua's efforts to make progress. But for some scenes, I don't think it is necessary to exaggerate too much. Moreover, the windows and doors inevitably show traces. In short, among the products of small companies, the expressive skills of "The Bell Rings" are still commendable. From this, it can be seen that the skills of Chinese films are indeed improving, which is a very gratifying fact.

Movie Actors Perform Stage Plays 249

It is not uncommon for movie actors to go on stage. Zhou Boxun's appearance in "High Society" was not long ago. Now that spring has come, it is again the season for performing plays. Many movie actors will be active on the stage. It is said that the stage play performance hosted by the Chinese Women's Cultural Society will have many movie actors participating in the performance, which will naturally be a big sensation again.

"Woman" Nears Completion 250

The screenplay and direction of "Woman" by Shi Dongshan, the female lead roles of Liming Hui and Hu Ping, and the male lead roles of Wang Yin and Wang Naidong have all achieved excellent results. The beauty of the pictures and the magnificence of the scenery are also rare in Chinese films. Zhou Kefang and Pei Lin have had great success in this film, and the director's attention to small movements in some scenes is also very interesting. It has now been filmed to eight-tenths, and it can be completely filmed in the shortest time.

Movie Novel

Carolina (10) 251

— Wen Yin

When Jonna heard Lee Qu's words, she almost cried. She said that when her father died, Mrs. Connery had personally promised to let her stay there. Lee Qu said: "That's no use either. The land is hers. You don't have a contract or agreement. If she wants to let you live, she will let you live: if she doesn't want to let you live, you will have to leave, you can't do what you want. Also, the money I lent you before, I'm afraid I can't rely on it now. In order to protect my own interests, I have to ask you for collateral. Didn't I tell you before that I didn't dare to go against Mrs. Connery?" After he finished speaking, he went to entertain other customers. Jonna had no choice but to come out with her head down. As Jonna left, Lee Qu looked at her over the top of his glasses and said, "I think you should go see Mr. Will." Jonna said, "Mr. Will is out." Lee Qu shrugged his shoulders and said, "That's right... he went to Charleston... to get married!"

In Charleston, marriage... Will was a little doubtful, but Virginia's intentions were too obvious. Today's banquet, tomorrow's

dance, money flowed like water on him, but he didn't seem to have much impression. Sometimes Virginia deliberately showed some affection, which made him uncomfortable and he had to deal with her perfunctorily. He kissed her, but felt nothing. One night, after the masquerade ball was over, Will held Virginia in his arms. She whispered to Will: "You look like you're not very well-behaved in that devil's costume." Will hugged her tightly and said, "I myself feel a little unruly." So they kissed and were intoxicated. In both of their hearts, it seemed like they had already tacitly agreed.

However, these were all temporary temptations and impulses. So the next day, Will felt awake, and he felt a little upset when he thought of what happened last night. He went to find Virginia and apologized to her very sincerely. He said: "I can't deceive you anymore. To tell you the truth, I really can't do this to the end. I also can't ask you to find a way to borrow money for us... I can't... I really like you... very much... but I love someone else... I can't marry you..." What he said was very sincere and should have moved a kind-hearted woman, but Virginia, although her smile remained the same, her eyes were already filled with dangerous dark clouds. She said: "Who mentioned marrying or not marrying you? That's probably still your personal delusion." Will called out "Virginia" and wanted to say something, but Virginia snorted and said, "You can go to the devil, you and your tenant's daughter, and those few acres of barren land!"

That day, Jonna ran back from the grocery store and went to seek an audience with Mrs. Connery. Mrs. Connery didn't want to see her, so she asked Gilatine to tell her that she wouldn't see her. Old Robert was also there, and his strange eyes stared at her without blinking, saying: "Oh, you're leaving?" Jonna said, "This is very difficult." She pleaded to Gilatine again: "Miss Gilatine, please go and tell Mrs. Connery. I have two younger brothers to take care of. Please let me see her and explain to her. If she asks me to leave before the tobacco is harvested, the owner of the new goods store will sell all my belongings..." (To be continued)
